Configure STT behavior for different use cases and languages.

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/flutter/stt/options#model-selection)

Model Selection
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Choose the right model based on your needs:

| Model | Size | Languages | Quality | Speed | Use Case |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `whisper-tiny.en` | ~75MB | English | Good | Fastest | Quick commands |
| `whisper-base.en` | ~150MB | English | Better | Fast | General use |
| `whisper-small.en` | ~250MB | English | Best | Medium | Accuracy-critical |
| `whisper-tiny` | ~75MB | Multi | Good | Fast | Multilingual apps |

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/flutter/stt/options#register-multiple-models)

Register Multiple Models
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Copy

Ask AI

    // English-optimized for primary use
    Onnx.addModel(
      id: 'whisper-tiny-en',
      name: 'Whisper Tiny English',
      url: 'https://github.com/RunanywhereAI/sherpa-onnx/releases/download/runanywhere-models-v1/sherpa-onnx-whisper-tiny.en.tar.gz',
      modality: ModelCategory.speechRecognition,
    );
    
    // Multilingual for international users
    Onnx.addModel(
      id: 'whisper-tiny-multi',
      name: 'Whisper Tiny Multilingual',
      url: 'https://github.com/RunanywhereAI/sherpa-onnx/releases/download/runanywhere-models-v1/sherpa-onnx-whisper-tiny.tar.gz',
      modality: ModelCategory.speechRecognition,
    );
    

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/flutter/stt/options#switch-models-at-runtime)

Switch Models at Runtime
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Copy

Ask AI

    // Load English model by default
    await RunAnywhere.loadSTTModel('whisper-tiny-en');
    
    // Switch to multilingual when needed
    Future<void> switchToMultilingual() async {
      await RunAnywhere.unloadSTTModel();
      await RunAnywhere.loadSTTModel('whisper-tiny-multi');
    }
    

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/flutter/stt/options#memory-management)

Memory Management
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Unload STT model when not needed to free memory:

Copy

Ask AI

    // Check if loaded
    if (RunAnywhere.isSTTModelLoaded) {
      print('Current STT model: ${RunAnywhere.currentSTTModelId}');
    }
    
    // Unload to free memory
    await RunAnywhere.unloadSTTModel();
    

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/flutter/stt/options#audio-preprocessing-tips)

Audio Preprocessing Tips
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Sample Rate Conversion

If your audio isn‚Äôt 16kHz, convert it before transcription: `dart // Example: Convert 44.1kHz to 16kHz // Use a package like 'flutter_sound' for resampling`

Noise Reduction

For noisy environments, consider preprocessing audio: - Apply a high-pass filter to remove low-frequency noise - Normalize audio levels - Remove silence at beginning/end

Audio Format

Always ensure correct format: - PCM16 (16-bit signed integer) - 16,000 Hz sample rate - Mono (single channel)

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/flutter/stt/options#error-handling)

Error Handling
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Copy

Ask AI

    try {
      final text = await RunAnywhere.transcribe(audioBytes);
      print('Transcribed: $text');
    } on SDKError catch (e) {
      switch (e.code) {
        case SDKErrorCode.sttNotAvailable:
          print('STT not available. Load an STT model first.');
          break;
        case SDKErrorCode.componentNotReady:
          print('STT model not loaded.');
          break;
        default:
          print('STT error: ${e.message}');
      }
    }
    

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/flutter/stt/options#best-practices)

Best Practices
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Start with the smallest model** that meets your accuracy needs. You can always upgrade later if needed.

1.  **Preload during idle time** ‚Äî Download and load STT model before user needs it
2.  **Use English-specific models** ‚Äî They‚Äôre smaller and more accurate for English
3.  **Handle empty audio** ‚Äî Check audio length before transcribing
4.  **Provide feedback** ‚Äî Show transcription progress to users

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/flutter/stt/options#see-also)

Kotlin SDK

Installation

On this page

*   [Gradle Setup](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/installation#gradle-setup)

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/installation#gradle-setup)

Gradle Setup
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Add the RunAnywhere SDK to your module-level `build.gradle.kts`:

build.gradle.kts (Module: app)

Copy

Ask AI

    dependencies {
        // Core SDK (required)
        implementation("com.runanywhere.sdk:runanywhere-kotlin:0.1.4")
    
        // LLM support - llama.cpp backend (~34MB)
        implementation("com.runanywhere.sdk:runanywhere-core-llamacpp:0.1.4")
    
        // STT/TTS/VAD support - ONNX backend (~25MB)
        implementation("com.runanywhere.sdk:runanywhere-core-onnx:0.1.4")
    }
    

Include only the modules you need. Each native module adds to your APK size: - **runanywhere-core-llamacpp**: ~34MB (for LLM text generation) - **runanywhere-core-onnx**: ~25MB (for STT, TTS, and VAD)

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/installation#module-overview)

Module Overview
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Module | Size | Features |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `runanywhere-kotlin` | ~2MB | Core SDK, model management, events |
| `runanywhere-core-llamacpp` | ~34MB | LLM text generation (GGUF models) |
| `runanywhere-core-onnx` | ~25MB | STT, TTS, VAD (ONNX models) |

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/installation#supported-model-formats)

Supported Model Formats
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Format | Extension | Backend | Use Case |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| GGUF | `.gguf` | llama.cpp | LLM text generation |
| ONNX | `.onnx` | ONNX Runtime | STT, TTS, VAD |
| ORT | `.ort` | ONNX Runtime | Optimized STT/TTS |

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/installation#android-manifest)

Android Manifest
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Add the required permissions to your `AndroidManifest.xml`:

AndroidManifest.xml

Copy

Ask AI

    <uses-permission android:name="android.permission.INTERNET" />
    <uses-permission android:name="android.permission.RECORD_AUDIO" />
    

`INTERNET` is required for model downloads. `RECORD_AUDIO` is only needed if you‚Äôre using STT or VAD with microphone input.

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/installation#proguard-rules)

ProGuard Rules
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If using ProGuard/R8 minification, add these rules:

proguard-rules.pro

Copy

Ask AI

    -keep class com.runanywhere.sdk.** { *; }
    -keepclassmembers class com.runanywhere.sdk.** { *; }

# System Prompts - RunAnywhere Documentation

[Skip to main content](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/flutter/llm/system-prompts#content-area)

[RunAnywhere Documentation home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/runanywhere/LBew9r1yliJTxAIH/logo-gradient.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=LBew9r1yliJTxAIH&q=85&s=8321e635ba8217e2714200582a9b09a8)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/runanywhere/LBew9r1yliJTxAIH/logo-gradient.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=LBew9r1yliJTxAIH&q=85&s=8321e635ba8217e2714200582a9b09a8)](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/)

Search...

‚åòKAsk AI

Search...

Navigation

LLM (Language Models)

System Prompts

On this page

*   [Basic Usage](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/flutter/llm/system-prompts#basic-usage)
    
*   [Common Patterns](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/flutter/llm/system-prompts#common-patterns)
    
*   [Coding Assistant](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/flutter/llm/system-prompts#coding-assistant)
    
*   [Customer Support Bot](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/flutter/llm/system-prompts#customer-support-bot)
    
*   [JSON Output](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/flutter/llm/system-prompts#json-output)
    
*   [Character/Persona](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/flutter/llm/system-prompts#character%2Fpersona)
    
*   [Tips for Effective System Prompts](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/flutter/llm/system-prompts#tips-for-effective-system-prompts)
    
*   [Reusable Prompt Class](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/flutter/llm/system-prompts#reusable-prompt-class)
    
*   [See Also](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/flutter/llm/system-prompts#see-also)
    

System prompts set the context and behavior for your AI model. Use them to create specialized assistants, enforce response formats, or constrain the model‚Äôs persona.

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/flutter/llm/system-prompts#basic-usage)

Basic Usage
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Copy

Ask AI

    final result = await RunAnywhere.generate(
      'Write a function to sort an array',
      options: LLMGenerationOptions(
        maxTokens: 300,
        systemPrompt: 'You are a helpful coding assistant. Write clean, well-commented code.',
      ),
    );
    

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/flutter/llm/system-prompts#common-patterns)

Common Patterns
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/flutter/llm/system-prompts#coding-assistant)

Coding Assistant

Copy

Ask AI

    const codingPrompt = '''
    You are an expert programmer. Follow these rules:
    - Write clean, readable code with comments
    - Use best practices and design patterns
    - Explain your approach briefly before the code
    - Handle edge cases
    ''';
    
    final result = await RunAnywhere.generate(
      'Implement a binary search in Dart',
      options: LLMGenerationOptions(
        systemPrompt: codingPrompt,
        maxTokens: 400,
      ),
    );
    

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/flutter/llm/system-prompts#customer-support-bot)

Customer Support Bot

Copy

Ask AI

    const supportPrompt = '''
    You are a friendly customer support agent for TechCorp.
    - Be helpful and empathetic
    - Keep responses concise (2-3 sentences)
    - If you don't know something, say so
    - Never make up information about products
    ''';
    

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/flutter/llm/system-prompts#json-output)

JSON Output

Copy

Ask AI

    const jsonPrompt = '''
    You are a data extraction assistant.
    Always respond with valid JSON only, no additional text.
    Extract the requested information into the specified format.
    ''';
    
    final result = await RunAnywhere.generate(
      'Extract: "John Smith, 25 years old, engineer at Google"',
      options: LLMGenerationOptions(
        systemPrompt: jsonPrompt,
        maxTokens: 100,
        temperature: 0.1,  // Lower temperature for consistent format
      ),
    );
    
    // Parse the JSON response
    final data = jsonDecode(result.text);
    

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/flutter/llm/system-prompts#character/persona)

Character/Persona

Copy

Ask AI

    const personaPrompt = '''
    You are Captain Nova, a space explorer from the year 3000.
    - Speak with enthusiasm about space and technology
    - Reference your adventures across the galaxy
    - Use occasional space-themed expressions
    - Stay in character at all times
    ''';
    

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/flutter/llm/system-prompts#tips-for-effective-system-prompts)

Tips for Effective System Prompts
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Be Specific

Vague prompts lead to inconsistent results. Specify exactly what you want: ‚ùå ‚ÄúBe helpful‚Äù ‚úÖ ‚ÄúProvide step-by-step instructions. Use bullet points. Keep each step under 20 words.‚Äù

Use Examples

Show the model what you expect: `Format responses like this example: Q: What is 2+2? A: **4** ‚Äî Two plus two equals four.`

Set Boundaries

Tell the model what NOT to do: `- Do not provide medical advice - Do not generate harmful content - If asked about topics outside your expertise, politely decline`

Keep It Concise

Shorter prompts use fewer tokens and leave more room for generation: ‚ùå Long, rambling instructions with repetition ‚úÖ Clear, bullet-pointed rules

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/flutter/llm/system-prompts#reusable-prompt-class)

Reusable Prompt Class
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Create a helper class for managing prompts:

Copy

Ask AI

    class SystemPrompts {
      static const String coding = '''
    You are an expert programmer. Write clean, well-documented code.
    ''';
    
      static const String creative = '''
    You are a creative writing assistant. Be imaginative and engaging.
    ''';
    
      static String forDomain(String domain) => '''
    You are an expert in $domain. Provide accurate, helpful information.
    ''';
    }
    
    // Usage
    final result = await RunAnywhere.generate(
      prompt,
      options: LLMGenerationOptions(
        systemPrompt: SystemPrompts.coding,
      ),
    );
    

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/flutter/llm/system-prompts#see-also)

# synthesize() - RunAnywhere Documentation

[Skip to main content](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/flutter/tts/synthesize#content-area)

TTS (Text-to-Speech)

synthesize()

On this page

*   [Basic Usage](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/flutter/tts/synthesize#basic-usage)
    
*   [TTSResult](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/flutter/tts/synthesize#ttsresult)
    
*   [Parameters](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/flutter/tts/synthesize#parameters)
    
*   [Setup](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/flutter/tts/synthesize#setup)
    
*   [1\. Register ONNX Backend](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/flutter/tts/synthesize#1-register-onnx-backend)
    
*   [2\. Add TTS Voice](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/flutter/tts/synthesize#2-add-tts-voice)
    
*   [3\. Download & Load](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/flutter/tts/synthesize#3-download-%26-load)
    
*   [Playing Audio](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/flutter/tts/synthesize#playing-audio)
    
*   [Complete Example](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/flutter/tts/synthesize#complete-example)
    
*   [See Also](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/flutter/tts/synthesize#see-also)
    

Synthesize natural-sounding speech from text using on-device Piper TTS models.

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/flutter/tts/synthesize#basic-usage)

Basic Usage
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Copy

Ask AI

    // Load a TTS voice
    await RunAnywhere.loadTTSVoice('vits-piper-en_US-lessac-medium');
    
    // Synthesize speech
    final result = await RunAnywhere.synthesize(
      'Hello! Welcome to RunAnywhere.',
      rate: 1.0,
      pitch: 1.0,
    );
    
    // result.samples contains PCM Float32 audio
    // result.sampleRate is typically 22050 Hz
    print('Duration: ${result.durationSeconds}s');
    

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/flutter/tts/synthesize#ttsresult)

TTSResult
------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Property | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `samples` | `Float32List` | Audio samples (PCM float) |
| `sampleRate` | `int` | Sample rate in Hz (typically 22050) |
| `durationMs` | `int` | Duration in milliseconds |
| `durationSeconds` | `double` | Duration in seconds |
| `numSamples` | `int` | Number of audio samples |

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/flutter/tts/synthesize#parameters)

Parameters
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Default | Description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `rate` | `double` | 1.0 | Speech rate (0.5 to 2.0) |
| `pitch` | `double` | 1.0 | Voice pitch (0.5 to 2.0) |
| `volume` | `double` | 1.0 | Volume (0.0 to 1.0) |

Copy

Ask AI

    // Slower, lower pitch for emphasis
    final result = await RunAnywhere.synthesize(
      'Important announcement!',
      rate: 0.8,
      pitch: 0.9,
      volume: 1.0,
    );
    

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/flutter/tts/synthesize#setup)

1\. Register ONNX Backend

Copy

Ask AI

    import 'package:runanywhere_onnx/runanywhere_onnx.dart';
    
    await Onnx.register();
    

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/flutter/tts/synthesize#2-add-tts-voice)

2\. Add TTS Voice

Copy

Ask AI

    Onnx.addModel(
      id: 'vits-piper-en_US-lessac-medium',
      name: 'Piper US English (Lessac)',
      url: 'https://github.com/RunanywhereAI/sherpa-onnx/releases/download/runanywhere-models-v1/vits-piper-en_US-lessac-medium.tar.bz2',
      modality: ModelCategory.textToSpeech,
    );
    

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/flutter/tts/synthesize#3-download-&-load)

3\. Download & Load

Copy

Ask AI

    // Download
    await for (final progress in RunAnywhere.downloadModel('vits-piper-en_US-lessac-medium')) {
      print('${(progress.percentage * 100).toStringAsFixed(1)}%');
      if (progress.state.isCompleted) break;
    }
    
    // Load
    await RunAnywhere.loadTTSVoice('vits-piper-en_US-lessac-medium');
    

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/flutter/tts/synthesize#playing-audio)

Playing Audio
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Use a package like `audioplayers` to play the synthesized audio:

Copy

Ask AI

    import 'package:audioplayers/audioplayers.dart';
    
    final player = AudioPlayer();
    
    Future<void> speakText(String text) async {
      final result = await RunAnywhere.synthesize(text);
    
      // Convert Float32 samples to bytes for playback
      final bytes = _convertToBytes(result.samples, result.sampleRate);
    
      // Play using audioplayers
      await player.play(BytesSource(bytes));
    }
    
    Uint8List _convertToBytes(Float32List samples, int sampleRate) {
      // Convert Float32 PCM to Int16 PCM WAV format
      final int16Samples = Int16List(samples.length);
      for (var i = 0; i < samples.length; i++) {
        int16Samples[i] = (samples[i] * 32767).clamp(-32768, 32767).toInt();
      }
    
      // Create WAV header + data
      return _createWavFile(int16Samples, sampleRate);
    }
    

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/flutter/tts/synthesize#complete-example)

Complete Example
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Copy

Ask AI

    class TextToSpeechDemo extends StatefulWidget {
      @override
      _TextToSpeechDemoState createState() => _TextToSpeechDemoState();
    }
    
    class _TextToSpeechDemoState extends State<TextToSpeechDemo> {
      final _controller = TextEditingController();
      final _player = AudioPlayer();
      bool _isSpeaking = false;
      bool _isLoaded = false;
    
      @override
      void initState() {
        super.initState();
        _initTTS();
      }
    
      Future<void> _initTTS() async {
        // Download if needed
        final models = await RunAnywhere.availableModels();
        final ttsModel = models.firstWhere(
          (m) => m.id == 'vits-piper-en_US-lessac-medium',
        );
    
        if (!ttsModel.isDownloaded) {
          await for (final p in RunAnywhere.downloadModel(ttsModel.id)) {
            if (p.state.isCompleted) break;
          }
        }
    
        // Load voice
        await RunAnywhere.loadTTSVoice('vits-piper-en_US-lessac-medium');
        setState(() => _isLoaded = true);
      }
    
      Future<void> _speak() async {
        if (_controller.text.isEmpty) return;
    
        setState(() => _isSpeaking = true);
    
        try {
          final result = await RunAnywhere.synthesize(_controller.text);
          // Play audio (implementation depends on your audio setup)
          await _playAudio(result);
        } finally {
          setState(() => _isSpeaking = false);
        }
      }
    
      @override
      Widget build(BuildContext context) {
        return Column(
          children: [\
            TextField(\
              controller: _controller,\
              decoration: InputDecoration(\
                hintText: 'Enter text to speak...',\
              ),\
              maxLines: 3,\
            ),\
            SizedBox(height: 16),\
            ElevatedButton.icon(\
              onPressed: _isLoaded && !_isSpeaking ? _speak : null,\
              icon: Icon(_isSpeaking ? Icons.stop : Icons.volume_up),\
              label: Text(_isSpeaking ? 'Speaking...' : 'Speak'),\
            ),\
          ],
        );
      }
    
      @override
      void dispose() {
        _controller.dispose();
        _player.dispose();
        super.dispose();
      }
    }

 to get started immediately with a full-featured demo app.

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/flutter/quick-start#complete-example)

Complete Example
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Here‚Äôs a complete example to get you started with on-device text generation:

Copy

Ask AI

    import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
    import 'package:runanywhere/runanywhere.dart';
    import 'package:runanywhere_llamacpp/runanywhere_llamacpp.dart';
    
    void main() async {
      WidgetsFlutterBinding.ensureInitialized();
    
      // 1. Initialize SDK
      await RunAnywhere.initialize();
    
      // 2. Register LlamaCpp backend
      await LlamaCpp.register();
    
      // 3. Add a model
      LlamaCpp.addModel(
        id: 'smollm2-360m-q8_0',
        name: 'SmolLM2 360M Q8_0',
        url: 'https://huggingface.co/prithivMLmods/SmolLM2-360M-GGUF/resolve/main/SmolLM2-360M.Q8_0.gguf',
        memoryRequirement: 500000000,
      );
    
      runApp(const MyApp());
    }
    
    class MyApp extends StatelessWidget {
      const MyApp({super.key});
    
      @override
      Widget build(BuildContext context) {
        return MaterialApp(
          home: ChatScreen(),
        );
      }
    }
    
    class ChatScreen extends StatefulWidget {
      @override
      _ChatScreenState createState() => _ChatScreenState();
    }
    
    class _ChatScreenState extends State<ChatScreen> {
      String _response = '';
      bool _isLoading = false;
      bool _isModelLoaded = false;
    
      Future<void> _loadModel() async {
        setState(() => _isLoading = true);
    
        try {
          // Download model (with progress)
          await for (final progress in RunAnywhere.downloadModel('smollm2-360m-q8_0')) {
            print('Download: ${(progress.percentage * 100).toStringAsFixed(1)}%');
            if (progress.state.isCompleted) break;
          }
    
          // Load model
          await RunAnywhere.loadModel('smollm2-360m-q8_0');
          setState(() => _isModelLoaded = true);
        } catch (e) {
          setState(() => _response = 'Error: $e');
        } finally {
          setState(() => _isLoading = false);
        }
      }
    
      Future<void> _generateText() async {
        setState(() => _isLoading = true);
    
        try {
          final result = await RunAnywhere.generate(
            'Explain quantum computing in simple terms',
            options: LLMGenerationOptions(
              maxTokens: 200,
              temperature: 0.7,
            ),
          );
    
          setState(() => _response = result.text);
          print('Speed: ${result.tokensPerSecond.toStringAsFixed(1)} tok/s');
        } catch (e) {
          setState(() => _response = 'Error: $e');
        } finally {
          setState(() => _isLoading = false);
        }
      }
    
      @override
      Widget build(BuildContext context) {
        return Scaffold(
          appBar: AppBar(title: Text('RunAnywhere Demo')),
          body: Padding(
            padding: EdgeInsets.all(16),
            child: Column(
              children: [\
                if (!_isModelLoaded)\
                  ElevatedButton(\
                    onPressed: _isLoading ? null : _loadModel,\
                    child: Text(_isLoading ? 'Loading...' : 'Download & Load Model'),\
                  ),\
                if (_isModelLoaded)\
                  ElevatedButton(\
                    onPressed: _isLoading ? null : _generateText,\
                    child: Text(_isLoading ? 'Generating...' : 'Generate'),\
                  ),\
                SizedBox(height: 20),\
                Expanded(\
                  child: SingleChildScrollView(\
                    child: Text(_response),\
                  ),\
                ),\
              ],
            ),
          ),
        );
      }
    }
    

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/flutter/quick-start#step-by-step-breakdown)

Step-by-Step Breakdown
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/flutter/quick-start#1-initialize-the-sdk)

1\. Initialize the SDK

Copy

Ask AI

    await RunAnywhere.initialize();
    

Initialize once at app startup. Development mode requires no API key.

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/flutter/quick-start#2-register-backend-modules)

2\. Register Backend Modules

Copy

Ask AI

    await LlamaCpp.register();  // For LLM
    await Onnx.register();      // For STT/TTS (optional)
    

Register the backends you need. Each backend is a separate package.

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/flutter/quick-start#3-register-models)

3\. Register Models

Copy

Ask AI

    LlamaCpp.addModel(
      id: 'smollm2-360m-q8_0',
      name: 'SmolLM2 360M Q8_0',
      url: 'https://huggingface.co/.../SmolLM2-360M.Q8_0.gguf',
      memoryRequirement: 500000000,
    );
    

Register models with their download URLs. Models are downloaded on-demand.

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/flutter/quick-start#4-download-&-load-models)

4\. Download & Load Models

Copy

Ask AI

    // Download with progress tracking
    await for (final progress in RunAnywhere.downloadModel('smollm2-360m-q8_0')) {
      print('${(progress.percentage * 100).toStringAsFixed(1)}%');
      if (progress.state.isCompleted) break;
    }
    
    // Load into memory
    await RunAnywhere.loadModel('smollm2-360m-q8_0');
    

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/flutter/quick-start#5-generate-text)

5\. Generate Text

Copy

Ask AI

    // Simple chat
    final response = await RunAnywhere.chat('Hello!');
    
    // Full generation with metrics
    final result = await RunAnywhere.generate(
      'Your prompt here',
      options: LLMGenerationOptions(maxTokens: 200),
    );
    print('Response: ${result.text}');
    print('Speed: ${result.tokensPerSecond} tok/s');
    

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/flutter/quick-start#environment-options)

Environment Options
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Environment | Description | API Key Required |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `.development` | Verbose logging, local-only | No  |
| `.staging` | Testing with real services | Yes |
| `.production` | Minimal logging, telemetry | Yes |

Copy

Ask AI

    // Production initialization
    await RunAnywhere.initialize(
      apiKey: 'your-api-key',
      baseURL: 'https://api.runanywhere.ai',
      environment: SDKEnvironment.production,
    );

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/introduction#overview)

Overview
-------------------------------------------------------------------------

The **RunAnywhere Kotlin SDK** is a production-grade, on-device AI SDK for Android. It enables developers to run AI models directly on Android devices without requiring network connectivity for inference, ensuring minimal latency and maximum privacy for your users. The SDK provides a unified interface to multiple AI capabilities:

[LLM\
---\
\
Text generation with streaming support via Kotlin Flows](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/llm/chat)
[STT\
---\
\
Speech-to-text transcription with Whisper models](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/stt/transcribe)
[TTS\
---\
\
Neural voice synthesis with Sherpa-ONNX](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/tts/synthesize)
[VAD\
---\
\
Real-time voice activity detection](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/vad)

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/introduction#key-capabilities)

Key Capabilities
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   **Multi-backend architecture** ‚Äì Choose from LlamaCPP (GGUF models) or ONNX Runtime
*   **GPU acceleration** ‚Äì Hardware-accelerated inference on supported devices
*   **Kotlin-first** ‚Äì Built with Coroutines and Flows for async operations
*   **Production-ready** ‚Äì Built-in analytics, logging, and model lifecycle management

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/introduction#core-philosophy)

Core Philosophy
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

On-Device First

All AI inference runs locally, ensuring low latency and data privacy. Once models are downloaded, no network connection is required for inference.

Modular Architecture

Backend engines are optional modules‚Äîinclude only what you need. This keeps your APK size minimal.

Privacy by Design

Audio and text data never leaves the device unless explicitly configured. Only anonymous analytics are collected by default.

Platform Parity

API mirrors the iOS Swift SDK for consistent cross-platform development.

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/introduction#features)

Features
-------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/introduction#language-models-llm)

Language Models (LLM)

*   On-device text generation with streaming support
*   Kotlin Flow-based token streaming
*   System prompts and customizable generation parameters
*   Support for thinking/reasoning models
*   LlamaCPP backend for GGUF models

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/introduction#speech-to-text-stt)

Speech-to-Text (STT)

*   Real-time streaming transcription
*   Batch audio transcription
*   Multi-language support
*   Whisper-based models via ONNX Runtime

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/introduction#text-to-speech-tts)

Text-to-Speech (TTS)

*   Neural voice synthesis with Sherpa-ONNX
*   System voices via Android TTS
*   Streaming audio generation for long text
*   Customizable voice, pitch, rate, and volume

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/introduction#voice-activity-detection-vad)

Voice Activity Detection (VAD)

*   Energy-based speech detection with Silero VAD
*   Configurable sensitivity thresholds
*   Real-time audio stream processing

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/introduction#voice-agent-pipeline)

Voice Agent Pipeline

*   Full VAD ‚Üí STT ‚Üí LLM ‚Üí TTS orchestration
*   Complete voice conversation flow
*   Streaming and batch processing modes

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/introduction#system-requirements)

System Requirements
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Platform | Minimum Version |
| --- | --- |
| Android | API 24 (7.0+) |

**Kotlin:** 2.0+ **Gradle:** 8.0+

ARM64 devices are recommended for best performance. GPU acceleration provides significant speedups on supported devices.

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/introduction#sdk-modules)

SDK Modules
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Module | Purpose |
| --- | --- |
| `runanywhere-core` | Core SDK (required) |
| `runanywhere-llamacpp` | LLM text generation with GGUF models |
| `runanywhere-onnx` | STT/TTS/VAD via ONNX Runtime |

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/introduction#architecture)

# transcribe() - RunAnywhere Documentation

[Skip to main content](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/flutter/stt/transcribe#content-area)

[RunAnywhere Documentation home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/runanywhere/LBew9r1yliJTxAIH/logo-gradient.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=LBew9r1yliJTxAIH&q=85&s=8321e635ba8217e2714200582a9b09a8)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/runanywhere/LBew9r1yliJTxAIH/logo-gradient.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=LBew9r1yliJTxAIH&q=85&s=8321e635ba8217e2714200582a9b09a8)](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/)

STT (Speech-to-Text)

transcribe()

On this page

*   [Basic Usage](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/flutter/stt/transcribe#basic-usage)
    
*   [With Detailed Result](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/flutter/stt/transcribe#with-detailed-result)
    
*   [STTResult](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/flutter/stt/transcribe#sttresult)
    
*   [Setup](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/flutter/stt/transcribe#setup)
    
*   [1\. Register ONNX Backend](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/flutter/stt/transcribe#1-register-onnx-backend)
    
*   [2\. Add STT Model](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/flutter/stt/transcribe#2-add-stt-model)
    
*   [3\. Download & Load](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/flutter/stt/transcribe#3-download-%26-load)
    
*   [Audio Format Requirements](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/flutter/stt/transcribe#audio-format-requirements)
    
*   [Recording Audio](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/flutter/stt/transcribe#recording-audio)
    
*   [Available Models](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/flutter/stt/transcribe#available-models)
    
*   [Complete Example](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/flutter/stt/transcribe#complete-example)
    
*   [See Also](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/flutter/stt/transcribe#see-also)
    

Transcribe audio data to text using on-device Whisper models via ONNX Runtime.

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/flutter/stt/transcribe#basic-usage)

Basic Usage
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Copy

Ask AI

    // Load STT model first
    await RunAnywhere.loadSTTModel('sherpa-onnx-whisper-tiny.en');
    
    // Transcribe audio data (PCM16 at 16kHz mono)
    final text = await RunAnywhere.transcribe(audioBytes);
    print('Transcription: $text');
    

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/flutter/stt/transcribe#with-detailed-result)

With Detailed Result
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Get confidence scores and metadata with `transcribeWithResult()`:

Copy

Ask AI

    final result = await RunAnywhere.transcribeWithResult(audioBytes);
    
    print('Text: ${result.text}');
    print('Confidence: ${(result.confidence * 100).toStringAsFixed(1)}%');
    print('Duration: ${result.durationMs}ms');
    if (result.language != null) {
      print('Language: ${result.language}');
    }
    

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/flutter/stt/transcribe#sttresult)

STTResult
------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Property | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `text` | `String` | Transcribed text |
| `confidence` | `double` | Confidence score (0.0 to 1.0) |
| `durationMs` | `int` | Audio duration in milliseconds |
| `language` | `String?` | Detected language code |

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/flutter/stt/transcribe#setup)

Setup
----------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/flutter/stt/transcribe#1-register-onnx-backend)

1\. Register ONNX Backend

Copy

Ask AI

    import 'package:runanywhere_onnx/runanywhere_onnx.dart';
    
    await Onnx.register();
    

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/flutter/stt/transcribe#2-add-stt-model)

2\. Add STT Model

Copy

Ask AI

    Onnx.addModel(
      id: 'sherpa-onnx-whisper-tiny.en',
      name: 'Whisper Tiny English',
      url: 'https://github.com/RunanywhereAI/sherpa-onnx/releases/download/runanywhere-models-v1/sherpa-onnx-whisper-tiny.en.tar.gz',
      modality: ModelCategory.speechRecognition,
    );
    

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/flutter/stt/transcribe#3-download-&-load)

3\. Download & Load

Copy

Ask AI

    // Download
    await for (final progress in RunAnywhere.downloadModel('sherpa-onnx-whisper-tiny.en')) {
      print('${(progress.percentage * 100).toStringAsFixed(1)}%');
      if (progress.state.isCompleted) break;
    }
    
    // Load
    await RunAnywhere.loadSTTModel('sherpa-onnx-whisper-tiny.en');
    

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/flutter/stt/transcribe#audio-format-requirements)

Audio Format Requirements
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Audio must be in the correct format for accurate transcription.

| Property | Required Value |
| --- | --- |
| Format | PCM (raw audio) |
| Sample Rate | 16,000 Hz (16kHz) |
| Channels | 1 (mono) |
| Bit Depth | 16-bit |

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/flutter/stt/transcribe#recording-audio)

Recording Audio
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Use a package like `record` to capture audio:

Copy

Ask AI

    import 'package:record/record.dart';
    
    final recorder = AudioRecorder();
    
    // Start recording with correct format
    await recorder.start(
      const RecordConfig(
        encoder: AudioEncoder.pcm16bits,
        sampleRate: 16000,
        numChannels: 1,
      ),
      path: tempFilePath,
    );
    
    // Stop and get audio
    await recorder.stop();
    final audioBytes = await File(tempFilePath).readAsBytes();
    
    // Transcribe
    final text = await RunAnywhere.transcribe(audioBytes);
    

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/flutter/stt/transcribe#available-models)

Available Models
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Model ID | Size | Languages | Speed |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `sherpa-onnx-whisper-tiny.en` | ~75MB | English | Fast |
| `sherpa-onnx-whisper-base.en` | ~150MB | English | Medium |
| `sherpa-onnx-whisper-small.en` | ~250MB | English | Slower |
| `sherpa-onnx-whisper-tiny` | ~75MB | Multilingual | Fast |

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/flutter/stt/transcribe#complete-example)

Complete Example
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Copy

Ask AI

    class TranscriptionDemo extends StatefulWidget {
      @override
      _TranscriptionDemoState createState() => _TranscriptionDemoState();
    }
    
    class _TranscriptionDemoState extends State<TranscriptionDemo> {
      final _recorder = AudioRecorder();
      String _transcription = '';
      bool _isRecording = false;
      bool _isTranscribing = false;
    
      Future<void> _toggleRecording() async {
        if (_isRecording) {
          // Stop and transcribe
          final path = await _recorder.stop();
          if (path != null) {
            setState(() {
              _isRecording = false;
              _isTranscribing = true;
            });
    
            final audioBytes = await File(path).readAsBytes();
            final text = await RunAnywhere.transcribe(audioBytes);
    
            setState(() {
              _transcription = text;
              _isTranscribing = false;
            });
          }
        } else {
          // Start recording
          if (await _recorder.hasPermission()) {
            final tempDir = await getTemporaryDirectory();
            final path = '${tempDir.path}/recording.pcm';
    
            await _recorder.start(
              const RecordConfig(
                encoder: AudioEncoder.pcm16bits,
                sampleRate: 16000,
                numChannels: 1,
              ),
              path: path,
            );
    
            setState(() => _isRecording = true);
          }
        }
      }
    
      @override
      Widget build(BuildContext context) {
        return Column(
          children: [\
            Text(_transcription),\
            ElevatedButton(\
              onPressed: _isTranscribing ? null : _toggleRecording,\
              child: Text(_isRecording ? 'Stop' : 'Record'),\
            ),\
            if (_isTranscribing) CircularProgressIndicator(),\
          ],
        );
      }
    }
    

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/flutter/stt/transcribe#see-also)

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/error-handling#sdkerror)

SDKError
---------------------------------------------------------------------------

All SDK operations throw `SDKError` for error conditions:

Copy

Ask AI

    data class SDKError(
        val code: ErrorCode,           // Specific error type
        val category: ErrorCategory,   // Error group
        val message: String,           // Human-readable message
        val cause: Throwable?          // Underlying exception
    ) : Exception(message, cause)
    

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/error-handling#basic-error-handling)

Basic Error Handling
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Copy

Ask AI

    try {
        RunAnywhere.loadLLMModel("my-model")
        val result = RunAnywhere.generate("Hello")
    
    } catch (e: SDKError) {
        when (e.code) {
            ErrorCode.NOT_INITIALIZED -> {
                showError("Please restart the app")
            }
            ErrorCode.MODEL_NOT_FOUND -> {
                showError("Model not found. Please download it first.")
            }
            ErrorCode.MODEL_LOAD_FAILED -> {
                showError("Failed to load model: ${e.message}")
            }
            ErrorCode.LLM_GENERATION_FAILED -> {
                showError("Generation failed: ${e.message}")
            }
            ErrorCode.INSUFFICIENT_STORAGE -> {
                showError("Not enough storage space")
            }
            else -> {
                showError(e.message ?: "Unknown error")
            }
        }
    }
    

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/error-handling#error-categories)

Error Categories
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Handle errors by category for broader matching:

Copy

Ask AI

    try {
        // SDK operations...
    } catch (e: SDKError) {
        when (e.category) {
            ErrorCategory.INITIALIZATION -> {
                // SDK not properly initialized
                restartApp()
            }
            ErrorCategory.MODEL -> {
                // Model-related issues
                promptModelDownload()
            }
            ErrorCategory.LLM -> {
                // Text generation errors
                retryWithSmallerPrompt()
            }
            ErrorCategory.STT -> {
                // Speech recognition errors
                checkMicrophonePermission()
            }
            ErrorCategory.TTS -> {
                // Speech synthesis errors
                checkAudioOutput()
            }
            ErrorCategory.NETWORK -> {
                // Network connectivity issues
                showOfflineMessage()
            }
            ErrorCategory.STORAGE -> {
                // Storage/file system errors
                promptStorageCleanup()
            }
            else -> {
                logError(e)
                showGenericError()
            }
        }
    }
    

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/error-handling#error-categories-reference)

Error Categories Reference
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Category | Description | Common Errors |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `INITIALIZATION` | SDK startup | `NOT_INITIALIZED`, `ALREADY_INITIALIZED` |
| `MODEL` | Model operations | `MODEL_NOT_FOUND`, `MODEL_LOAD_FAILED` |
| `LLM` | Text generation | `LLM_GENERATION_FAILED` |
| `STT` | Speech-to-text | `STT_TRANSCRIPTION_FAILED` |
| `TTS` | Text-to-speech | `TTS_SYNTHESIS_FAILED` |
| `VAD` | Voice detection | `VAD_DETECTION_FAILED` |
| `NETWORK` | Network issues | `NETWORK_UNAVAILABLE`, `TIMEOUT` |
| `DOWNLOAD` | Model downloads | `DOWNLOAD_FAILED`, `DOWNLOAD_CANCELLED` |
| `STORAGE` | Storage issues | `INSUFFICIENT_STORAGE`, `FILE_NOT_FOUND` |

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/error-handling#common-error-codes)

Common Error Codes
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Copy

Ask AI

    enum class ErrorCode {
        // General
        SUCCESS,
        UNKNOWN,
        INVALID_ARGUMENT,
    
        // Initialization
        NOT_INITIALIZED,
        ALREADY_INITIALIZED,
    
        // Model
        MODEL_NOT_FOUND,
        MODEL_NOT_LOADED,
        MODEL_LOAD_FAILED,
    
        // LLM
        LLM_GENERATION_FAILED,
    
        // STT
        STT_TRANSCRIPTION_FAILED,
    
        // TTS
        TTS_SYNTHESIS_FAILED,
    
        // VAD
        VAD_DETECTION_FAILED,
    
        // Network
        NETWORK_ERROR,
        NETWORK_UNAVAILABLE,
        TIMEOUT,
    
        // Download
        DOWNLOAD_FAILED,
        DOWNLOAD_CANCELLED,
    
        // Storage
        INSUFFICIENT_STORAGE,
        FILE_NOT_FOUND,
        OUT_OF_MEMORY
    }
    

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/error-handling#error-factory-methods)

Error Factory Methods
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Create specific errors programmatically:

Copy

Ask AI

    // These are used internally by the SDK
    SDKError.modelNotFound(modelId)
    SDKError.modelNotLoaded(modelId)
    SDKError.modelLoadFailed(modelId, reason)
    SDKError.llmGenerationFailed(reason)
    SDKError.sttTranscriptionFailed(reason)
    SDKError.ttsSynthesisFailed(reason)
    SDKError.networkUnavailable()
    SDKError.timeout(operation, timeoutMs)
    SDKError.insufficientStorage(requiredBytes)
    SDKError.fileNotFound(path)
    

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/error-handling#example-comprehensive-error-handler)

Example: Comprehensive Error Handler
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Copy

Ask AI

    class SDKErrorHandler {
    
        fun handle(error: SDKError, context: Context) {
            Log.e("SDK", "Error: ${error.code} - ${error.message}", error.cause)
    
            val userMessage = when (error.code) {
                // Initialization errors
                ErrorCode.NOT_INITIALIZED ->
                    "The AI system isn't ready yet. Please wait or restart the app."
    
                // Model errors
                ErrorCode.MODEL_NOT_FOUND ->
                    "This model isn't available. Please download it first."
                ErrorCode.MODEL_LOAD_FAILED ->
                    "Couldn't load the AI model. Try freeing up some memory."
    
                // Generation errors
                ErrorCode.LLM_GENERATION_FAILED ->
                    "Couldn't generate a response. Please try again."
                ErrorCode.STT_TRANSCRIPTION_FAILED ->
                    "Couldn't understand the audio. Please speak clearly."
                ErrorCode.TTS_SYNTHESIS_FAILED ->
                    "Couldn't create audio. Please try again."
    
                // Network errors
                ErrorCode.NETWORK_UNAVAILABLE ->
                    "No internet connection. Some features may be limited."
                ErrorCode.TIMEOUT ->
                    "Request took too long. Please try again."
    
                // Download errors
                ErrorCode.DOWNLOAD_FAILED ->
                    "Download failed. Please check your connection and try again."
                ErrorCode.DOWNLOAD_CANCELLED ->
                    "Download was cancelled."
    
                // Storage errors
                ErrorCode.INSUFFICIENT_STORAGE ->
                    "Not enough storage space. Free up some space and try again."
                ErrorCode.OUT_OF_MEMORY ->
                    "Not enough memory. Try closing other apps."
    
                else ->
                    "Something went wrong. Please try again."
            }
    
            Toast.makeText(context, userMessage, Toast.LENGTH_LONG).show()
        }
    }
    

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/error-handling#subscribe-to-error-events)

Subscribe to Error Events
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Copy

Ask AI

    lifecycleScope.launch {
        RunAnywhere.events.errorEvents.collect { errorEvent ->
            Log.e("SDK", "Error event: ${errorEvent.code} - ${errorEvent.message}")
            // Handle or report error
        }
    }
    

[Configuration](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/configuration)

# chat() - RunAnywhere Documentation

[Skip to main content](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/llm/chat#content-area)

[RunAnywhere Documentation home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/runanywhere/LBew9r1yliJTxAIH/logo-gradient.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=LBew9r1yliJTxAIH&q=85&s=8321e635ba8217e2714200582a9b09a8)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/runanywhere/LBew9r1yliJTxAIH/logo-gradient.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=LBew9r1yliJTxAIH&q=85&s=8321e635ba8217e2714200582a9b09a8)](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/)

LLM (Language Models)

chat()

On this page

*   [When to Use](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/llm/chat#when-to-use)
    
*   [Example: Simple Q&A](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/llm/chat#example-simple-q%26a)
    
*   [Example: Chat Bot](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/llm/chat#example-chat-bot)
    

The simplest way to generate text‚Äîa single function call that returns the response directly.

Copy

Ask AI

    // One-liner for quick responses
    val response = RunAnywhere.chat("What is the capital of France?")
    println(response)  // "The capital of France is Paris."
    

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/llm/chat#when-to-use)

When to Use
---------------------------------------------------------------------------

Use `chat()` when you need:

*   Quick, simple responses
*   No metrics or metadata
*   Minimal code

For more control, use [`generate()`](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/llm/generate)
 or [`generateStream()`](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/llm/stream)
.

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/llm/chat#example-simple-q&a)

Example: Simple Q&A
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Copy

Ask AI

    lifecycleScope.launch {
        try {
            val answer = RunAnywhere.chat("Explain machine learning in one sentence")
            textView.text = answer
        } catch (e: SDKError) {
            showError(e.message)
        }
    }
    

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/llm/chat#example-chat-bot)

Example: Chat Bot
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Copy

Ask AI

    suspend fun sendMessage(userMessage: String): String {
        // Ensure model is loaded
        if (!RunAnywhere.isLLMModelLoaded()) {
            RunAnywhere.loadLLMModel(modelId)
        }
    
        return RunAnywhere.chat(userMessage)
    }
    

`chat()` uses default generation options. For custom temperature, max tokens, or system prompts, use [`generate()`](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/llm/generate)
 instead.

[Quick Start](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/quick-start)
[generate()](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/llm/generate)

# generate() - RunAnywhere Documentation

[Skip to main content](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/llm/generate#content-area)

[RunAnywhere Documentation home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/runanywhere/LBew9r1yliJTxAIH/logo-gradient.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=LBew9r1yliJTxAIH&q=85&s=8321e635ba8217e2714200582a9b09a8)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/runanywhere/LBew9r1yliJTxAIH/logo-gradient.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=LBew9r1yliJTxAIH&q=85&s=8321e635ba8217e2714200582a9b09a8)](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/)

Search...

‚åòKAsk AI

Search...

Navigation

LLM (Language Models)

generate()

On this page

*   [LLMGenerationResult](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/llm/generate#llmgenerationresult)
    
*   [LLMGenerationOptions](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/llm/generate#llmgenerationoptions)
    
*   [Example: Creative Writing](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/llm/generate#example-creative-writing)
    
*   [Example: Factual Response](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/llm/generate#example-factual-response)
    
*   [Cancel Generation](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/llm/generate#cancel-generation)
    

Use `generate()` for full control over text generation with detailed performance metrics.

Copy

Ask AI

    val result = RunAnywhere.generate(
        prompt = "Write a haiku about Kotlin programming",
        options = LLMGenerationOptions(
            maxTokens = 50,
            temperature = 1.0f,
            topP = 0.9f,
            stopSequences = listOf("###")
        )
    )
    
    println("Response: ${result.text}")
    println("Model: ${result.modelUsed}")
    println("Tokens: ${result.tokensUsed}")
    println("Speed: ${result.tokensPerSecond} tok/s")
    println("Latency: ${result.latencyMs}ms")
    
    // For reasoning models (e.g., models with thinking capability)
    result.thinkingContent?.let { thinking ->
        println("Reasoning: $thinking")
    }
    

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/llm/generate#llmgenerationresult)

LLMGenerationResult
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The result object contains comprehensive metrics:

| Property | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `text` | `String` | Generated response text |
| `thinkingContent` | `String?` | Reasoning content (for thinking models) |
| `inputTokens` | `Int` | Number of prompt tokens |
| `tokensUsed` | `Int` | Number of output tokens |
| `modelUsed` | `String` | Model ID used for generation |
| `latencyMs` | `Double` | Total generation time in milliseconds |
| `tokensPerSecond` | `Double` | Generation speed |
| `timeToFirstTokenMs` | `Double?` | Time to first token (streaming) |
| `framework` | `String?` | Inference framework used |

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/llm/generate#llmgenerationoptions)

LLMGenerationOptions
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Customize generation behavior:

Copy

Ask AI

    data class LLMGenerationOptions(
        val maxTokens: Int = 100,           // Maximum tokens to generate
        val temperature: Float = 0.8f,      // Creativity (0.0-2.0)
        val topP: Float = 1.0f,             // Nucleus sampling (0.0-1.0)
        val stopSequences: List<String> = emptyList(),
        val streamingEnabled: Boolean = false,
        val systemPrompt: String? = null    // System behavior prompt
    )
    

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/llm/generate#example-creative-writing)

Example: Creative Writing
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Copy

Ask AI

    val story = RunAnywhere.generate(
        prompt = "Write a short story about a robot learning to paint",
        options = LLMGenerationOptions(
            maxTokens = 500,
            temperature = 1.2f,   // Higher = more creative
            topP = 0.95f
        )
    )
    

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/llm/generate#example-factual-response)

Example: Factual Response
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Copy

Ask AI

    val facts = RunAnywhere.generate(
        prompt = "List the planets in our solar system",
        options = LLMGenerationOptions(
            maxTokens = 200,
            temperature = 0.1f,   // Lower = more deterministic
            topP = 0.5f
        )
    )
    

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/llm/generate#cancel-generation)

Cancel Generation
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Cancel an ongoing generation:

Copy

Ask AI

    // Start generation in a coroutine
    val job = lifecycleScope.launch {
        val result = RunAnywhere.generate(longPrompt, options)
    }
    
    // Cancel if needed
    cancelButton.setOnClickListener {
        RunAnywhere.cancelGeneration()
        job.cancel()
    }
    

[chat()](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/llm/chat)
[generateStream()](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/llm/stream)

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/react-native/introduction#overview)

Overview
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The **RunAnywhere React Native SDK** is a production-grade, on-device AI SDK for React Native applications. It enables developers to run AI models directly on iOS and Android devices without requiring network connectivity for inference, ensuring minimal latency and maximum privacy for your users. The SDK provides a unified interface to multiple AI capabilities:

[LLM\
---\
\
Text generation with streaming support via async iterators](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/react-native/llm/chat)
[STT\
---\
\
Speech-to-text transcription with Whisper models](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/react-native/stt/transcribe)
[TTS\
---\
\
Neural voice synthesis with Piper TTS](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/react-native/tts/synthesize)
[VAD\
---\
\
Real-time voice activity detection with Silero VAD](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/react-native/vad)

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/react-native/introduction#key-capabilities)

Key Capabilities
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   **Multi-backend architecture** ‚Äì Choose from LlamaCPP (GGUF models) or ONNX Runtime
*   **Cross-platform** ‚Äì Single codebase for iOS and Android
*   **TypeScript-first** ‚Äì Full type safety and IDE autocomplete
*   **Production-ready** ‚Äì Built-in analytics, logging, and model lifecycle management

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/react-native/introduction#core-philosophy)

Core Philosophy
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

On-Device First

All AI inference runs locally, ensuring low latency and data privacy. Once models are downloaded, no network connection is required for inference.

Modular Architecture

Backend engines are optional packages‚Äîinclude only what you need. This keeps your app bundle size minimal.

Privacy by Design

Audio and text data never leaves the device unless explicitly configured. Only anonymous analytics are collected by default.

Platform Parity

API mirrors the iOS Swift SDK and Android Kotlin SDK for consistent cross-platform development.

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/react-native/introduction#features)

Features
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/react-native/introduction#language-models-llm)

Language Models (LLM)

*   On-device text generation with streaming support
*   Async iterator-based token streaming
*   System prompts and customizable generation parameters
*   Support for thinking/reasoning models
*   LlamaCPP backend for GGUF models

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/react-native/introduction#speech-to-text-stt)

Speech-to-Text (STT)

*   Real-time streaming transcription
*   Batch audio transcription
*   Multi-language support
*   Whisper-based models via ONNX Runtime

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/react-native/introduction#text-to-speech-tts)

Text-to-Speech (TTS)

*   Neural voice synthesis with Piper TTS
*   System voices via platform TTS
*   Streaming audio generation for long text
*   Customizable voice, pitch, rate, and volume

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/react-native/introduction#voice-activity-detection-vad)

Voice Activity Detection (VAD)

*   Energy-based speech detection with Silero VAD
*   Configurable sensitivity thresholds
*   Real-time audio stream processing

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/react-native/introduction#voice-agent-pipeline)

Voice Agent Pipeline

*   Full VAD ‚Üí STT ‚Üí LLM ‚Üí TTS orchestration
*   Complete voice conversation flow
*   Push-to-talk and hands-free modes

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/react-native/introduction#system-requirements)

System Requirements
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Platform | Minimum Version |
| --- | --- |
| React Native | 0.74+ |
| iOS | 15.1+ |
| Android | API 24 (7.0+) |

**Node.js:** 18+ **TypeScript:** 5.0+ (recommended)

Apple Silicon devices (M1/M2/M3, A14+) and Android devices with 6GB+ RAM are recommended. Metal GPU acceleration provides 3-5x speedup on iOS.

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/react-native/introduction#multi-package-architecture)

Multi-Package Architecture
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Package | Purpose |
| --- | --- |
| `@runanywhere/core` | Core SDK (required) |
| `@runanywhere/llamacpp` | LLM text generation with GGUF models |
| `@runanywhere/onnx` | STT/TTS/VAD via ONNX Runtime |

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/react-native/introduction#architecture)

Architecture
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

     ‚Äì Bare React Native CLI app with Chat, STT, TTS, and Voice Pipeline demos

Swift SDK

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/swift/installation#swift-package-manager-xcode)

Swift Package Manager (Xcode)
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1

[](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/swift/installation#)

Open your project

Open your project in Xcode

2

[](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/swift/installation#)

Add package dependency

Go to **File ‚Üí Add Package Dependencies‚Ä¶**

3

[](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/swift/installation#)

Enter repository URL

Enter the repository URL: `https://github.com/RunanywhereAI/runanywhere-sdks`

4

[](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/swift/installation#)

Select version

Select the version (e.g., `from: "0.16.0"`)

5

[](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/swift/installation#)

Choose products

Choose the products you need: - **RunAnywhere** (required) ‚Äì Core SDK - **RunAnywhereLlamaCPP** ‚Äì LLM text generation with GGUF models - **RunAnywhereONNX** ‚Äì ONNX Runtime for STT/TTS/VAD

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/swift/installation#package-swift)

Package.swift
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

For Swift packages, add the dependency directly to your `Package.swift`:

Package.swift

Copy

Ask AI

    dependencies: [\
        .package(url: "https://github.com/RunanywhereAI/runanywhere-sdks", from: "0.16.0")\
    ]
    

Then add the products you need to your target dependencies:

Package.swift

Copy

Ask AI

    targets: [\
        .target(\
            name: "YourApp",\
            dependencies: [\
                .product(name: "RunAnywhere", package: "runanywhere-sdks"),\
                .product(name: "RunAnywhereLlamaCPP", package: "runanywhere-sdks"),\
                .product(name: "RunAnywhereONNX", package: "runanywhere-sdks"),\
            ]\
        )\
    ]
    

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/swift/installation#available-products)

Available Products
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Product | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `RunAnywhere` | Core SDK (required for all features) |
| `RunAnywhereLlamaCPP` | LLM capability with GGUF models |
| `RunAnywhereONNX` | STT, TTS, and VAD via ONNX Runtime |

Only include the products you need to minimize your app‚Äôs binary size. The modular architecture means you can add capabilities incrementally.

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/swift/installation#binary-size-impact)

Binary Size Impact
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Configuration | Approximate Size |
| --- | --- |
| LLM only | ~17 MB |
| STT only (ONNX) | ~52 MB |
| LLM + STT + TTS | ~87 MB |
| Full (all backends) | ~95 MB |

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/swift/installation#verify-installation)

Verify Installation
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

After installation, verify everything is working:

Copy

Ask AI

    import RunAnywhere
    
    // Check SDK version
    print("SDK Version: \(RunAnywhere.version)")
    

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/swift/installation#troubleshooting)

Troubleshooting
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Package resolution fails

Try resetting package caches: 1. Go to **File ‚Üí Packages ‚Üí Reset Package Caches** 2. Clean the build folder: **Product ‚Üí Clean Build Folder** 3. Try adding the package again

Module not found errors

Ensure you‚Äôve added the correct product to your target‚Äôs dependencies. Each module must be explicitly added.

Linker errors with XCFrameworks

If you encounter linker errors, ensure your deployment target meets the minimum requirements: - iOS 17.0+ - macOS 14.0+

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/swift/installation#next-steps)

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/best-practices#memory-management)

Memory Management
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

On-device AI models are memory-intensive. Proper memory management is critical for app stability.

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/best-practices#load-only-what-you-need)

Load Only What You Need

Copy

Ask AI

    // ‚ùå Don't load multiple large models
    RunAnywhere.loadLLMModel("model-3b")
    RunAnywhere.loadSTTModel("whisper-large")
    
    // ‚úÖ Load one LLM at a time, use smaller models
    RunAnywhere.loadLLMModel("model-0.5b")
    

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/best-practices#unload-when-not-needed)

Unload When Not Needed

Copy

Ask AI

    // Unload models when switching tasks or backgrounding
    override fun onStop() {
        super.onStop()
        lifecycleScope.launch {
            RunAnywhere.unloadLLMModel()
            RunAnywhere.unloadSTTModel()
        }
    }
    

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/best-practices#monitor-memory-before-loading)

Monitor Memory Before Loading

Copy

Ask AI

    val modelInfo = RunAnywhere.model(modelId)
    val requiredMemory = modelInfo?.downloadSize ?: 0
    
    val activityManager = getSystemService(Context.ACTIVITY_SERVICE) as ActivityManager
    val memoryInfo = ActivityManager.MemoryInfo()
    activityManager.getMemoryInfo(memoryInfo)
    
    if (memoryInfo.availMem < requiredMemory * 1.5) {
        showWarning("Low memory - performance may be affected")
    }
    

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/best-practices#performance-optimization)

Performance Optimization
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/best-practices#use-quantized-models)

Use Quantized Models

| Model Type | Size | Performance | Quality |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Q8 (8-bit) | Larger | Slower | Best |
| Q4 (4-bit) | Smaller | Faster | Good |
| Q2 (2-bit) | Smallest | Fastest | Acceptable |

Copy

Ask AI

    // ‚úÖ Use Q4 models for mobile devices
    val model = RunAnywhere.registerModel(
        name = "Qwen 0.5B Q4",
        url = "...qwen2.5-0.5b-instruct-q4_0.gguf",
        framework = InferenceFramework.LLAMA_CPP
    )
    

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/best-practices#use-streaming-for-better-ux)

Use Streaming for Better UX

Copy

Ask AI

    // ‚úÖ Stream tokens for perceived faster responses
    RunAnywhere.generateStream(prompt)
        .collect { token ->
            textView.append(token)
        }
    
    // ‚ùå Waiting for full response feels slow
    val result = RunAnywhere.generate(prompt)
    textView.text = result.text
    

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/best-practices#set-appropriate-token-limits)

Set Appropriate Token Limits

Copy

Ask AI

    // ‚úÖ Match maxTokens to your use case
    val shortAnswer = LLMGenerationOptions(maxTokens = 50)   // Quick Q&A
    val mediumAnswer = LLMGenerationOptions(maxTokens = 200) // General chat
    val longForm = LLMGenerationOptions(maxTokens = 500)     // Stories/articles
    

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/best-practices#app-lifecycle)

App Lifecycle
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/best-practices#handle-background/foreground)

Handle Background/Foreground

Copy

Ask AI

    class MyApplication : Application(), LifecycleEventObserver {
    
        override fun onCreate() {
            super.onCreate()
            ProcessLifecycleOwner.get().lifecycle.addObserver(this)
            RunAnywhere.initialize(environment = SDKEnvironment.PRODUCTION)
        }
    
        override fun onStateChanged(source: LifecycleOwner, event: Lifecycle.Event) {
            when (event) {
                Lifecycle.Event.ON_STOP -> {
                    // App backgrounded - release resources
                    CoroutineScope(Dispatchers.Main).launch {
                        RunAnywhere.stopVoiceSession()
                        RunAnywhere.cleanup()
                    }
                }
                Lifecycle.Event.ON_START -> {
                    // App foregrounded - reinitialize if needed
                }
                else -> {}
            }
        }
    }
    

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/best-practices#preload-models-at-launch)

Preload Models at Launch

Copy

Ask AI

    class SplashActivity : AppCompatActivity() {
    
        override fun onCreate(savedInstanceState: Bundle?) {
            super.onCreate(savedInstanceState)
    
            lifecycleScope.launch {
                // Show loading UI
                showLoading()
    
                // Preload commonly used models
                val models = listOf("qwen-0.5b", "whisper-tiny")
    
                models.forEach { modelId ->
                    if (!RunAnywhere.isModelDownloaded(modelId)) {
                        RunAnywhere.downloadModel(modelId).collect { progress ->
                            updateProgress(modelId, progress.progress)
                        }
                    }
                }
    
                // Pre-load the primary model
                RunAnywhere.loadLLMModel("qwen-0.5b")
    
                // Navigate to main screen
                startActivity(Intent(this@SplashActivity, MainActivity::class.java))
                finish()
            }
        }
    }
    

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/best-practices#error-handling)

Error Handling
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/best-practices#always-handle-errors)

Always Handle Errors

Copy

Ask AI

    // ‚úÖ Comprehensive error handling
    lifecycleScope.launch {
        try {
            val result = RunAnywhere.generate(prompt)
            showResponse(result.text)
        } catch (e: SDKError) {
            when (e.category) {
                ErrorCategory.MODEL -> promptModelDownload()
                ErrorCategory.STORAGE -> promptStorageCleanup()
                else -> showGenericError(e.message)
            }
        }
    }
    

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/best-practices#provide-user-feedback)

Provide User Feedback

Copy

Ask AI

    // ‚úÖ Show meaningful progress
    RunAnywhere.downloadModel(modelId).collect { progress ->
        when (progress.state) {
            DownloadState.DOWNLOADING -> {
                progressBar.progress = (progress.progress * 100).toInt()
                statusText.text = "Downloading AI model..."
            }
            DownloadState.EXTRACTING -> {
                statusText.text = "Preparing model..."
            }
            DownloadState.COMPLETED -> {
                statusText.text = "Ready!"
            }
            DownloadState.ERROR -> {
                showError("Download failed: ${progress.error}")
            }
        }
    }

    // Simulators don't accurately reflect:

    // - CPU performance
    // - Thermal throttling
    // Always test on physical devices before release

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/best-practices#measure-performance)

Measure Performance

Copy

Ask AI

    val result = RunAnywhere.generate(prompt, options)
    
    Log.d("Performance", """
        Model: ${result.modelUsed}
        Tokens: ${result.tokensUsed}
        Speed: ${result.tokensPerSecond} tok/s
        Latency: ${result.latencyMs}ms
        TTFT: ${result.timeToFirstTokenMs}ms
    """.trimIndent())

    // ‚ùå Don't hardcode API keys

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/best-practices#summary-checklist)

Summary Checklist
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [ ]  Use quantized models (Q4) for mobile devices
*   [ ]  Unload models when backgrounding the app
*   [ ]  Use streaming for long text generation
*   [ ]  Handle all error categories appropriately
*   [ ]  Test on physical devices, not simulators
*   [ ]  Preload commonly used models at app startup
*   [ ]  Monitor memory before loading large models
*   [ ]  Secure API keys using BuildConfig or secure storage

[Error Handling](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/error-handling)
[Introduction](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/react-native/introduction)

‚åòI

# Streaming TTS - RunAnywhere Documentation

TTS (Text-to-Speech)

Streaming TTS

On this page

*   [Streaming Synthesis](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/tts/stream#streaming-synthesis)
    
*   [Example: Streaming Audio Player](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/tts/stream#example-streaming-audio-player)
    
*   [Example: Chat Response with Streaming TTS](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/tts/stream#example-chat-response-with-streaming-tts)
    
*   [Stop Synthesis](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/tts/stream#stop-synthesis)
    
*   [When to Use Streaming](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/tts/stream#when-to-use-streaming)
    
*   [Performance Characteristics](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/tts/stream#performance-characteristics)
    

Stream audio chunks as they are synthesized, enabling playback to start before the full synthesis completes.

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/tts/stream#streaming-synthesis)

Streaming Synthesis
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Copy

Ask AI

    val longText = """
        This is a very long text that will be synthesized in chunks.
        Each chunk will be delivered as soon as it's ready,
        allowing playback to start immediately without waiting
        for the entire synthesis to complete.
    """.trimIndent()
    
    RunAnywhere.synthesizeStream(
        text = longText,
        options = TTSOptions(rate = 1.0f),
        onAudioChunk = { chunk ->
            // Play each chunk as it arrives
            audioPlayer.enqueue(chunk)
        }
    )
    

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/tts/stream#example-streaming-audio-player)

Example: Streaming Audio Player
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Copy

Ask AI

    class StreamingAudioPlayer {
        private val audioQueue = ConcurrentLinkedQueue<ByteArray>()
        private var isPlaying = false
    
        fun enqueue(audioChunk: ByteArray) {
            audioQueue.add(audioChunk)
            if (!isPlaying) {
                startPlayback()
            }
        }
    
        private fun startPlayback() {
            isPlaying = true
            CoroutineScope(Dispatchers.IO).launch {
                while (audioQueue.isNotEmpty() || isPlaying) {
                    val chunk = audioQueue.poll()
                    if (chunk != null) {
                        playChunk(chunk)
                    } else {
                        delay(10) // Wait for more chunks
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    
        private fun playChunk(chunk: ByteArray) {
            // Play audio chunk using AudioTrack
        }
    
        fun stop() {
            isPlaying = false
            audioQueue.clear()
        }
    }
    

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/tts/stream#example-chat-response-with-streaming-tts)

Example: Chat Response with Streaming TTS
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Copy

Ask AI

    class ChatViewModel : ViewModel() {
        private val audioPlayer = StreamingAudioPlayer()
    
        fun sendMessageAndSpeak(prompt: String) {
            viewModelScope.launch {
                // Generate text with streaming
                val streamResult = RunAnywhere.generateStreamWithMetrics(prompt)
    
                // Collect full response for TTS
                val fullResponse = StringBuilder()
                streamResult.stream.collect { token ->
                    fullResponse.append(token)
                    _displayText.value += token
                }
    
                // Stream synthesize the full response
                RunAnywhere.synthesizeStream(
                    text = fullResponse.toString(),
                    options = TTSOptions(),
                    onAudioChunk = { chunk ->
                        audioPlayer.enqueue(chunk)
                    }
                )
            }
        }
    }
    

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/tts/stream#stop-synthesis)

Stop Synthesis
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Cancel ongoing synthesis:

Copy

Ask AI

    // Stop synthesis mid-stream
    RunAnywhere.stopSynthesis()
    

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/tts/stream#when-to-use-streaming)

When to Use Streaming
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Scenario | Recommended |
| --- | --- |
| Short text (under 100 chars) | `synthesize()` |
| Long text (over 200 chars) | `synthesizeStream()` |
| Real-time chat responses | `synthesizeStream()` |
| Pre-cached audio | `synthesize()` |

Streaming synthesis reduces time-to-first-audio for long text: - **Regular synthesis**: Wait for full synthesis, then play - **Streaming synthesis**: Start playing after first chunk (~100ms)

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/tts/stream#performance-characteristics)

Performance Characteristics
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Text Length | Regular Synthesis | Streaming First Audio |
| --- | --- | --- |
| 50 chars | ~100ms | ~100ms |
| 200 chars | ~400ms | ~100ms |
| 500 chars | ~1000ms | ~100ms |
| 1000 chars | ~2000ms | ~100ms |

[synthesize()](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/tts/synthesize)
[Voices](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/tts/voices)
