| **GPU Acceleration** | Metal | GPU | Native | Native |

* * *

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/sdks#choosing-the-right-sdk)

Choosing the Right SDK
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Building a native iOS/macOS app?

Use the **Swift SDK** for the best performance and access to Apple-specific features like Metal acceleration and Apple Foundation Models.[Get Started with Swift\
----------------------](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/swift/introduction)

Building a native Android app?

Use the **Kotlin SDK** for native Android performance with Coroutines-based async APIs and GPU acceleration.[Get Started with Kotlin\
-----------------------](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/introduction)

Building a cross-platform app with JavaScript/TypeScript?

Use the **React Native SDK** if your team is already using React Native. Get full type safety with TypeScript and a single codebase.[Get Started with React Native\
-----------------------------](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/react-native/introduction)

Building a cross-platform app with Flutter/Dart?

Use the **Flutter SDK** if your team is already using Flutter. Get native Dart APIs with async/await patterns.[Get Started with Flutter\
------------------------](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/flutter/introduction)

**Not sure which to choose?** All SDKs have feature parity. Pick the one that matches your existing tech stack for the smoothest integration.

[Quick Start](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/quickstart)
[Introduction](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/swift/introduction)

System prompts define how the model should behave, respond, and what role it should assume.

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/llm/system-prompts#basic-usage)

Basic Usage
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Copy

Ask AI

    val options = LLMGenerationOptions(
        maxTokens = 200,
        systemPrompt = """
            You are a senior Kotlin developer.
            Answer questions with code examples.
            Use modern Kotlin conventions and coroutines.
        """.trimIndent()
    )
    
    val result = RunAnywhere.generate(
        prompt = "How do I make an HTTP request?",
        options = options
    )
    

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/llm/system-prompts#example-code-assistant)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Copy

Ask AI

    val codeAssistant = LLMGenerationOptions(
        maxTokens = 500,
        temperature = 0.3f,  // Lower for more precise code
        systemPrompt = """
            You are an expert Android developer assistant.
            - Always provide working Kotlin code examples
            - Use Jetpack libraries when appropriate
            - Follow Material Design guidelines for UI code
            - Include error handling in your examples
            - Keep explanations concise
        """.trimIndent()
    )
    
    val result = RunAnywhere.generate(
        prompt = "How do I implement a RecyclerView with DiffUtil?",
        options = codeAssistant
    )

Example: JSON Output
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Copy

Ask AI

    val jsonFormatter = LLMGenerationOptions(
        maxTokens = 500,
        temperature = 0.1f,  // Very low for consistent structure
        systemPrompt = """
            You are a data extraction assistant.
            Always respond with valid JSON only.
            Do not include any text outside the JSON object.

        """.trimIndent()
    )

    )

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/llm/system-prompts#best-practices)

Best Practices
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Keep system prompts focused and specific:** - Define the role clearly - Set boundaries on what the model should/shouldn‚Äôt do - Specify output format if needed - Include examples for complex tasks

| Goal | Temperature | System Prompt Style |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Code generation | 0.1-0.4 | Precise, technical instructions |
| Creative writing | 0.9-1.3 | Open-ended, encourage creativity |
| Factual Q&A | 0.2-0.5 | Focus on accuracy, cite limitations |
| Conversation | 0.6-0.8 | Personality traits, response guidelines |

[generateStream()](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/llm/stream)
[transcribe()](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/stt/transcribe)

    val audioData = // ... recorded audio bytes

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/stt/stream#real-time-microphone-transcription)

Real-Time Microphone Transcription
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Copy

Ask AI

    class LiveTranscriptionViewModel : ViewModel() {
        private val _partialText = MutableStateFlow("")
        val partialText: StateFlow<String> = _partialText
    
        private val _finalText = MutableStateFlow("")
        val finalText: StateFlow<String> = _finalText
    
        fun processAudioSamples(samples: FloatArray) {
            viewModelScope.launch {
                // Process streaming audio samples
                RunAnywhere.processStreamingAudio(samples)
            }
        }
    
        fun stopTranscription() {
            viewModelScope.launch {
                RunAnywhere.stopStreamingTranscription()
            }
        }
    }
    

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/stt/stream#stream-audio-samples)

Stream Audio Samples
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

For continuous microphone input:

Copy

Ask AI

    // Start streaming transcription
    suspend fun startLiveTranscription(
        audioSamplesFlow: Flow<FloatArray>,
        onPartialResult: (String) -> Unit
    ) {
        audioSamplesFlow.collect { samples ->
            RunAnywhere.processStreamingAudio(samples)
            // Handle partial results via event system
        }
    }
    

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/stt/stream#subscribe-to-stt-events)

Subscribe to STT Events
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Use the event system for streaming updates:

Copy

Ask AI

    lifecycleScope.launch {
        RunAnywhere.events.sttEvents.collect { event ->
            when (event.eventType) {
                STTEventType.PARTIAL_RESULT -> {
                    event.transcript?.let { partial ->
                        partialTextView.text = partial
                    }
                }
                STTEventType.TRANSCRIPTION_COMPLETED -> {
                    event.transcript?.let { final ->
                        finalTextView.text = final
                    }
                }
                STTEventType.TRANSCRIPTION_FAILED -> {
                    showError(event.error ?: "Transcription failed")
                }
            }
        }
    }
    

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/stt/stream#example-voice-search)

Example: Voice Search
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Copy

Ask AI

    class VoiceSearchActivity : AppCompatActivity() {
        private lateinit var audioRecorder: AudioRecorder
    
        override fun onCreate(savedInstanceState: Bundle?) {
            super.onCreate(savedInstanceState)
    
            // Load STT model
            lifecycleScope.launch {
                RunAnywhere.loadSTTModel("whisper-tiny")
            }
    
            // Subscribe to transcription events
            lifecycleScope.launch {
                RunAnywhere.events.sttEvents.collect { event ->
                    if (event.eventType == STTEventType.PARTIAL_RESULT) {
                        searchInput.setText(event.transcript)
                    }
                }
            }
    
            micButton.setOnClickListener {
                if (isRecording) {
                    stopRecording()
                } else {
                    startRecording()
                }
            }
        }
    
        private fun startRecording() {
            audioRecorder.start { samples ->
                lifecycleScope.launch {
                    RunAnywhere.processStreamingAudio(samples)
                }
            }
        }
    
        private fun stopRecording() {
            audioRecorder.stop()
            lifecycleScope.launch {
                RunAnywhere.stopStreamingTranscription()
            }
        }
    }
    

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/stt/stream#performance-tips)

Performance Tips
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

For optimal streaming performance: - Process audio in chunks of 30-100ms - Use 16kHz sample rate for Whisper models - Consider using VAD to detect speech segments

| Use Case | Recommended Approach |
| --- | --- |
| Pre-recorded audio | `transcribe()` |
| Live microphone | `processStreamingAudio()` |
| Real-time dictation | Streaming + VAD |

[transcribe()](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/stt/transcribe)
[STT Options](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/stt/options)

Kotlin SDK

Voice Activity Detection

On this page

*   [Basic Usage](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/vad#basic-usage)
    
*   [VADResult](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/vad#vadresult)
    
*   [Configure VAD](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/vad#configure-vad)
    
*   [VADConfiguration](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/vad#vadconfiguration)
    
*   [Streaming VAD](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/vad#streaming-vad)
    
*   [Calibrate with Ambient Noise](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/vad#calibrate-with-ambient-noise)
    
*   [Example: Voice Recording with VAD](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/vad#example-voice-recording-with-vad)
    
*   [VAD Statistics](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/vad#vad-statistics)
    
*   [Reset VAD](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/vad#reset-vad)
    
*   [Best Practices](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/vad#best-practices)
    

Voice Activity Detection (VAD) identifies speech segments in audio streams, enabling responsive voice interfaces.

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/vad#basic-usage)

Basic Usage
----------------------------------------------------------------------

Copy

Ask AI

    // Detect speech in audio data
    val audioData: ByteArray = // ... from recording
    val result = RunAnywhere.detectVoiceActivity(audioData)
    
    if (result.hasSpeech) {
        println("Speech detected!")
        println("Confidence: ${result.confidence}")
    }
    

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/vad#vadresult)

VADResult
------------------------------------------------------------------

| Property | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `hasSpeech` | `Boolean` | Whether speech was detected |
| `confidence` | `Float` | Detection confidence (0.0-1.0) |
| `speechStartMs` | `Long?` | Start time of speech segment |
| `speechEndMs` | `Long?` | End time of speech segment |
| `frameIndex` | `Int` | Audio frame index |
| `timestamp` | `Long` | Detection timestamp |

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/vad#configure-vad)

Configure VAD
--------------------------------------------------------------------------

Customize detection sensitivity:

Copy

Ask AI

    RunAnywhere.configureVAD(VADConfiguration(
        threshold = 0.5f,              // Detection threshold (0.0-1.0)
        minSpeechDurationMs = 250,     // Minimum speech duration
        minSilenceDurationMs = 300,    // Silence before speech end
        sampleRate = 16000,            // Audio sample rate
        frameSizeMs = 30               // Frame size for processing
    ))
    

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/vad#vadconfiguration)

VADConfiguration
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Copy

Ask AI

    data class VADConfiguration(
        val threshold: Float = 0.5f,
        val minSpeechDurationMs: Int = 250,
        val minSilenceDurationMs: Int = 300,
        val sampleRate: Int = 16000,
        val frameSizeMs: Int = 30
    )
    

| Parameter | Default | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `threshold` | 0.5 | Higher = less sensitive (fewer false positives) |
| `minSpeechDurationMs` | 250 | Ignore speech shorter than this |
| `minSilenceDurationMs` | 300 | Silence needed to end speech |
| `sampleRate` | 16000 | Audio sample rate |
| `frameSizeMs` | 30  | Frame duration for processing |

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/vad#streaming-vad)

Streaming VAD
--------------------------------------------------------------------------

Process continuous audio with Kotlin Flows:

Copy

Ask AI

    // Create a flow of audio samples from microphone
    val audioSamplesFlow: Flow<FloatArray> = microphoneManager.audioFlow
    
    // Stream VAD results
    RunAnywhere.streamVAD(audioSamplesFlow)
        .collect { result ->
            if (result.hasSpeech) {
                updateUI(state = "Speaking...")
            } else {
                updateUI(state = "Listening...")
            }
        }
    

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/vad#calibrate-with-ambient-noise)

Calibrate with Ambient Noise
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Improve accuracy by calibrating with ambient noise:

Copy

Ask AI

    // Record a few seconds of ambient noise
    val ambientAudio = recordAmbientNoise(durationMs = 2000)
    
    // Calibrate VAD
    RunAnywhere.calibrateVAD(ambientAudio)
    

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/vad#example-voice-recording-with-vad)

Example: Voice Recording with VAD
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Copy

Ask AI

    class VoiceRecorderViewModel : ViewModel() {
        private val _isListening = MutableStateFlow(false)
        val isListening: StateFlow<Boolean> = _isListening
    
        private val _isSpeaking = MutableStateFlow(false)
        val isSpeaking: StateFlow<Boolean> = _isSpeaking
    
        private val audioBuffer = mutableListOf<FloatArray>()
    
        fun startListening(audioFlow: Flow<FloatArray>) {
            viewModelScope.launch {
                _isListening.value = true
    
                // Configure VAD
                RunAnywhere.configureVAD(VADConfiguration(
                    threshold = 0.5f,
                    minSpeechDurationMs = 300,
                    minSilenceDurationMs = 500
                ))
    
                // Stream VAD
                RunAnywhere.streamVAD(audioFlow)
                    .collect { result ->
                        _isSpeaking.value = result.hasSpeech
    
                        if (result.hasSpeech) {
                            // Buffer audio during speech
                            // (actual audio capture would be handled separately)
                        } else if (audioBuffer.isNotEmpty()) {
                            // Speech ended - process buffered audio
                            processRecordedAudio()
                        }
                    }
            }
        }
    
        fun stopListening() {
            viewModelScope.launch {
                _isListening.value = false
                RunAnywhere.resetVAD()
            }
        }
    
        private suspend fun processRecordedAudio() {
            // Convert buffer to ByteArray and transcribe
            val audioData = audioBuffer.toByteArray()
            val transcription = RunAnywhere.transcribe(audioData)
            _transcription.value = transcription
            audioBuffer.clear()
        }
    }
    

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/vad#vad-statistics)

VAD Statistics
----------------------------------------------------------------------------

Get current VAD performance metrics:

Copy

Ask AI

    val stats = RunAnywhere.getVADStatistics()
    println("Total frames processed: ${stats.framesProcessed}")
    println("Speech frames: ${stats.speechFrames}")
    println("Current state: ${stats.currentState}")
    

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/vad#reset-vad)

Reset VAD
------------------------------------------------------------------

Clear VAD state for a fresh start:

Copy

Ask AI

    RunAnywhere.resetVAD()
    

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/vad#best-practices)

Best Practices
----------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Calibration**: Always calibrate VAD with ambient noise for best results in noisy environments.**Threshold tuning**:

*   Quiet environment: threshold = 0.3-0.5
*   Noisy environment: threshold = 0.6-0.8

**Buffer management**: Use VAD to determine when to start/stop recording, but buffer audio slightly before speech detection for complete captures.

[Voices](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/tts/voices)
[Voice Agent](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/voice-agent)

STT (Speech-to-Text)

transcribe()

On this page

*   [Basic Transcription](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/stt/transcribe#basic-transcription)
    
*   [Transcription with Options](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/stt/transcribe#transcription-with-options)

*   [Supported Audio Formats](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/stt/transcribe#supported-audio-formats)
    

Transcribe audio data to text using on-device speech recognition models.

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/stt/transcribe#basic-transcription)

Basic Transcription
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Copy

Ask AI

    // Load an STT model first
    RunAnywhere.loadSTTModel("whisper-tiny")
    
    // Transcribe audio bytes
    val audioData: ByteArray = // ... from file or recording
    val text = RunAnywhere.transcribe(audioData)
    println(text)  // "Hello, how are you today?"
    

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/stt/transcribe#transcription-with-options)

Transcription with Options
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Get detailed output including confidence scores and timestamps:

Copy

Ask AI

    val output = RunAnywhere.transcribeWithOptions(
        audioData = audioBytes,
        options = STTOptions(
            language = "en",
            enableTimestamps = true,
            enablePunctuation = true
        )
    )
    
    println("Text: ${output.text}")
    println("Confidence: ${output.confidence}")
    
    // Access word-level timestamps
    output.wordTimestamps?.forEach { word ->
        println("[${word.startTime}s - ${word.endTime}s]: ${word.word}")
    }
    

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/stt/transcribe#sttoutput)

STTOutput
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------

The detailed output object:

| Property | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `text` | `String` | Transcribed text |
| `confidence` | `Float` | Confidence score (0.0-1.0) |
| `wordTimestamps` | `List<WordTimestamp>?` | Word-level timing |
| `detectedLanguage` | `String?` | Auto-detected language code |
| `metadata` | `TranscriptionMetadata` | Processing metrics |

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/stt/transcribe#example-transcribe-audio-file)

Example: Transcribe Audio File
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Copy

Ask AI

    suspend fun transcribeAudioFile(uri: Uri): String {
        val audioData = contentResolver.openInputStream(uri)?.readBytes()
            ?: throw IllegalArgumentException("Cannot read audio file")
    
        // Ensure STT model is loaded
        if (!RunAnywhere.isSTTModelLoaded()) {
            RunAnywhere.loadSTTModel("whisper-tiny")
        }
    
        return RunAnywhere.transcribe(audioData)
    }
    

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/stt/transcribe#example-record-and-transcribe)

Example: Record and Transcribe
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Copy

Ask AI

    class VoiceRecorderViewModel : ViewModel() {
        private var audioRecorder: AudioRecord? = null
        private val audioBuffer = mutableListOf<Byte>()
    
        fun startRecording() {
            // Start recording audio...
        }
    
        fun stopAndTranscribe() {
            viewModelScope.launch {
                val audioData = audioBuffer.toByteArray()
    
                val result = RunAnywhere.transcribeWithOptions(
                    audioData,
                    options = STTOptions(
                        language = "en",
                        enablePunctuation = true
                    )
                )
    
                _transcription.value = result.text
                _confidence.value = result.confidence
            }
        }
    }
    

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/stt/transcribe#model-management)

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/stt/transcribe#supported-audio-formats)

Supported Audio Formats
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Format | Sample Rate | Notes |
| --- | --- | --- |
| PCM | 16000 Hz | Recommended for best quality |
| WAV | 16000 Hz | Standard audio file format |
| MP3 | Any | Converted internally |

For best transcription accuracy: - Use 16kHz mono PCM audio - Keep audio clips under 30 seconds for optimal performance - Use a smaller model (whisper-tiny) for faster results, larger models (whisper-base) for better accuracy

[System Prompts](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/llm/system-prompts)
[Streaming STT](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/stt/stream)

LLM (Language Models)

generateStream()

On this page

*   [Basic Streaming](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/llm/stream#basic-streaming)
    
*   [Streaming with Metrics](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/llm/stream#streaming-with-metrics)
    
*   [LLMStreamingResult](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/llm/stream#llmstreamingresult)

*   [Example: Jetpack Compose Integration](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/llm/stream#example-jetpack-compose-integration)
    
*   [Performance Tips](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/llm/stream#performance-tips)
    

Use streaming for responsive UIs that display text as it‚Äôs generated, providing a better user experience for longer responses.

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/llm/stream#basic-streaming)

Basic Streaming
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Copy

Ask AI

    RunAnywhere.generateStream("Tell me a story about AI")
        .collect { token ->
            // Display each token as it arrives
            print(token)
            textView.append(token)
        }
    

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/llm/stream#streaming-with-metrics)

Streaming with Metrics
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Get both the token stream AND final metrics:

Copy

Ask AI

    val streamResult = RunAnywhere.generateStreamWithMetrics(
        prompt = "Explain quantum computing",
        options = LLMGenerationOptions(maxTokens = 500)
    )
    
    // Collect tokens as they arrive
    streamResult.stream.collect { token ->
        textView.append(token)
    }
    
    // Get final metrics after streaming completes
    val metrics = streamResult.result.await()
    println("\n\nGenerated ${metrics.tokensUsed} tokens")
    println("Speed: ${metrics.tokensPerSecond} tok/s")
    println("Time to first token: ${metrics.timeToFirstTokenMs}ms")
    

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/llm/stream#llmstreamingresult)

LLMStreamingResult
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Copy

Ask AI

    data class LLMStreamingResult(
        val stream: Flow<String>,                    // Token stream
        val result: Deferred<LLMGenerationResult>    // Final metrics (awaitable)
    )
    

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/llm/stream#example-chat-ui-with-streaming)

Example: Chat UI with Streaming
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Copy

Ask AI

    class ChatViewModel : ViewModel() {
        private val _currentResponse = MutableStateFlow("")
        val currentResponse: StateFlow<String> = _currentResponse
    
        private val _isGenerating = MutableStateFlow(false)
        val isGenerating: StateFlow<Boolean> = _isGenerating
    
        fun sendMessage(prompt: String) {
            viewModelScope.launch {
                _isGenerating.value = true
                _currentResponse.value = ""
    
                try {
                    RunAnywhere.generateStream(prompt)
                        .collect { token ->
                            _currentResponse.value += token
                        }
                } catch (e: Exception) {
                    _currentResponse.value = "Error: ${e.message}"
                } finally {
                    _isGenerating.value = false
                }
            }
        }
    
        fun cancelGeneration() {
            RunAnywhere.cancelGeneration()
        }
    }
    

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/llm/stream#example-jetpack-compose-integration)

Example: Jetpack Compose Integration
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Copy

Ask AI

    @Composable
    fun StreamingTextView(viewModel: ChatViewModel) {
        val response by viewModel.currentResponse.collectAsState()
        val isGenerating by viewModel.isGenerating.collectAsState()
    
        Column {
            Text(
                text = response,
                modifier = Modifier
                    .fillMaxWidth()
                    .padding(16.dp)
            )
    
            if (isGenerating) {
                LinearProgressIndicator(
                    modifier = Modifier.fillMaxWidth()
                )
            }
        }
    }
    

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/llm/stream#performance-tips)

Performance Tips
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Streaming provides better perceived performance for long generations: - **Time to First Token (TTFT)**: ~50-100ms - Users see immediate feedback instead of waiting for the full response

| Scenario | Recommended Approach |
| --- | --- |
| Short responses (under 50 tokens) | `generate()` |
| Long responses (over 100 tokens) | `generateStream()` |
| Chat interfaces | `generateStream()` |
| Background processing | `generate()` |

[generate()](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/llm/generate)
[System Prompts](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/llm/system-prompts)

‚åòI

Voice Configuration
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Customize voice parameters in TTSOptions:

Copy

Ask AI

    val options = TTSOptions(
        voice = "en-US-Neural2-F",   // Specific voice ID
        rate = 0.8f,                  // 0.0-2.0, slower speed
        pitch = 1.3f,                 // 0.0-2.0, higher pitch
        volume = 1.0f                 // 0.0-1.0
    )
    
    val output = RunAnywhere.synthesize("Hello world", options)
    

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/tts/voices#rate-pitch-and-volume)

Rate, Pitch, and Volume
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Range | Default | Effect |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `rate` | 0.0-2.0 | 1.0 | Speech speed (0.5 = half speed, 2.0 = double speed) |
| `pitch` | 0.0-2.0 | 1.0 | Voice pitch (lower = deeper, higher = lighter) |
| `volume` | 0.0-1.0 | 1.0 | Audio volume |

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/tts/voices#example-voice-selector)

Example: Voice Selector
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Copy

Ask AI

    class VoiceSelectorViewModel : ViewModel() {
        private val _availableVoices = MutableStateFlow<List<String>>(emptyList())
        val availableVoices: StateFlow<List<String>> = _availableVoices
    
        private val _selectedVoice = MutableStateFlow<String?>(null)
        val selectedVoice: StateFlow<String?> = _selectedVoice
    
        init {
            viewModelScope.launch {
                _availableVoices.value = RunAnywhere.availableTTSVoices()
            }
        }
    
        fun selectVoice(voiceId: String) {
            viewModelScope.launch {
                RunAnywhere.loadTTSVoice(voiceId)
                _selectedVoice.value = voiceId
            }
        }
    
        fun previewVoice(voiceId: String) {
            viewModelScope.launch {
                RunAnywhere.loadTTSVoice(voiceId)
                RunAnywhere.speak(
                    "Hello! This is a preview of the selected voice.",
                    TTSOptions(rate = 1.0f)
                )
            }
        }
    }
    

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/tts/voices#sherpa-onnx-voices)

Sherpa-ONNX Voices
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The SDK uses Sherpa-ONNX for neural TTS. Available voice packs include:

| Voice ID | Language | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `en-us-default` | English (US) | Default English voice |
| `en-gb-default` | English (UK) | British English voice |
| `de-de-default` | German | German voice |
| `fr-fr-default` | French | French voice |
| `es-es-default` | Spanish | Spanish voice |

Voice availability depends on downloaded voice models. Use `availableTTSVoices()` to see what‚Äôs available on the device.

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/tts/voices#download-additional-voices)

Download Additional Voices
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Register and download additional TTS voice models:

Copy

Ask AI

    // Register a TTS voice model
    val voiceModel = RunAnywhere.registerModel(
        name = "Piper English Amy",
        url = "https://example.com/piper-en-us-amy.onnx",
        framework = InferenceFramework.ONNX,
        modality = ModelCategory.SPEECH_SYNTHESIS
    )
    
    // Download the voice
    RunAnywhere.downloadModel(voiceModel.id).collect { progress ->
        println("Downloading: ${(progress.progress * 100).toInt()}%")
    }
    
    // Load and use
    RunAnywhere.loadTTSVoice(voiceModel.id)
    

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/tts/voices#best-practices)

Best Practices
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   **Preload voices** at app startup for instant TTS - **Use streaming** for long text to reduce latency - **Cache common phrases** as audio files for fastest playback - **Match voice language** to content language for best quality

[Streaming TTS](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/tts/stream)
[Voice Activity Detection](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/vad)

STT (Speech-to-Text)

STT Options

On this page

*   [STTOptions](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/stt/options#sttoptions)
    
*   [Configuration Examples](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/stt/options#configuration-examples)
    
*   [Basic English Transcription](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/stt/options#basic-english-transcription)
    
*   [Multi-Language Detection](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/stt/options#multi-language-detection)
    
*   [Transcription with Timestamps](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/stt/options#transcription-with-timestamps)
    
*   [Speaker Diarization](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/stt/options#speaker-diarization)
    
*   [Custom Vocabulary](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/stt/options#custom-vocabulary)
    
*   [Supported Languages](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/stt/options#supported-languages)
    
*   [AudioFormat](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/stt/options#audioformat)
    
*   [TranscriptionMetadata](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/stt/options#transcriptionmetadata)
    

Customize transcription behavior with `STTOptions`.

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/stt/options#sttoptions)

STTOptions
----------------------------------------------------------------------------

Copy

Ask AI

    data class STTOptions(
        val language: String = "en",              // BCP-47 language code
        val detectLanguage: Boolean = false,      // Auto-detect spoken language
        val enablePunctuation: Boolean = true,    // Add punctuation
        val enableDiarization: Boolean = false,   // Identify speakers
        val maxSpeakers: Int? = null,             // Max speakers to identify
        val enableTimestamps: Boolean = true,     // Word-level timestamps
        val vocabularyFilter: List<String> = emptyList(),  // Custom vocabulary
        val audioFormat: AudioFormat = AudioFormat.PCM,
        val sampleRate: Int = 16000               // Audio sample rate
    )
    

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/stt/options#configuration-examples)

Configuration Examples
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/stt/options#basic-english-transcription)

Basic English Transcription

Copy

Ask AI

    val options = STTOptions(
        language = "en",
        enablePunctuation = true
    )
    

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/stt/options#multi-language-detection)

Multi-Language Detection

Copy

Ask AI

    val options = STTOptions(
        detectLanguage = true,
        enablePunctuation = true
    )
    
    val result = RunAnywhere.transcribeWithOptions(audioData, options)
    println("Detected language: ${result.detectedLanguage}")
    

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/stt/options#transcription-with-timestamps)

Transcription with Timestamps

Copy

Ask AI

    val options = STTOptions(
        language = "en",
        enableTimestamps = true
    )
    
    val result = RunAnywhere.transcribeWithOptions(audioData, options)
    result.wordTimestamps?.forEach { word ->
        println("[${word.startTime}s - ${word.endTime}s]: ${word.word}")
    }
    

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/stt/options#speaker-diarization)

Speaker Diarization

Copy

Ask AI

    val options = STTOptions(
        language = "en",
        enableDiarization = true,
        maxSpeakers = 2
    )
    

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/stt/options#custom-vocabulary)

Custom Vocabulary

Improve recognition for domain-specific terms:

Copy

Ask AI

    val options = STTOptions(
        language = "en",
        vocabularyFilter = listOf(
            "RunAnywhere",
            "Kotlin",
            "ONNX",
            "llama.cpp"
        )
    )
    

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/stt/options#supported-languages)

Supported Languages
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Code | Language |
| --- | --- |
| `en` | English |
| `es` | Spanish |
| `fr` | French |
| `de` | German |
| `it` | Italian |
| `pt` | Portuguese |
| `zh` | Chinese |
| `ja` | Japanese |
| `ko` | Korean |

Language support depends on the STT model. Whisper models support 99+ languages.

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/stt/options#audioformat)

AudioFormat
------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Copy

Ask AI

    enum class AudioFormat {
        PCM,    // Raw PCM samples
        WAV,    // WAV container
        MP3,    // MP3 compressed
        AAC,    // AAC compressed
        OGG,    // Ogg Vorbis
        OPUS,   // Opus codec
        FLAC    // FLAC lossless
    }
    

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/stt/options#transcriptionmetadata)

TranscriptionMetadata
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Access processing metrics:

Copy

Ask AI

    val result = RunAnywhere.transcribeWithOptions(audioData, options)
    
    val metadata = result.metadata
    println("Model: ${metadata.modelId}")
    println("Processing time: ${metadata.processingTime}s")
    println("Audio length: ${metadata.audioLength}s")
    println("Real-time factor: ${metadata.realTimeFactor}x")
    

| Property | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `modelId` | STT model used |
| `processingTime` | Time to process (seconds) |
| `audioLength` | Input audio duration (seconds) |
| `realTimeFactor` | Processing time / audio length |

A real-time factor < 1.0 means the transcription is faster than real-time. For example, 0.2x means 10 seconds of audio processed in 2 seconds.

[Streaming STT](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/stt/stream)
[synthesize()](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/tts/synthesize)

‚åòI

Kotlin SDK

Quick Start

On this page

*   [Complete Example](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/quick-start#complete-example)
    
*   [Step-by-Step Guide](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/quick-start#step-by-step-guide)
    
*   [1\. Initialize the SDK](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/quick-start#1-initialize-the-sdk)
    
*   [Environment Options](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/quick-start#environment-options)
    
*   [2\. Register a Model](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/quick-start#2-register-a-model)
    
*   [3\. Download the Model](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/quick-start#3-download-the-model)
    
*   [4\. Load and Generate](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/quick-start#4-load-and-generate)
    
*   [5\. Stream Responses](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/quick-start#5-stream-responses)
    
*   [What‚Äôs Next?](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/quick-start#what%E2%80%99s-next)
    

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/quick-start#complete-example)

Complete Example
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Here‚Äôs a complete example to get you started with on-device text generation:

MainActivity.kt

Copy

Ask AI

    import com.runanywhere.sdk.public.RunAnywhere
    import com.runanywhere.sdk.public.SDKEnvironment
    import com.runanywhere.sdk.public.extensions.*
    import com.runanywhere.sdk.core.types.InferenceFramework
    
    class MyApplication : Application() {
        override fun onCreate() {
            super.onCreate()
    
            // 1. Initialize SDK (fast, ~1-5ms)
            RunAnywhere.initialize(
                apiKey = "your-api-key",    // Optional for development
                environment = SDKEnvironment.DEVELOPMENT
            )
        }
    }
    
    // 2. Use in your Activity/Fragment
    class MainActivity : AppCompatActivity() {
        private var modelId: String? = null
    
        override fun onCreate(savedInstanceState: Bundle?) {
            super.onCreate(savedInstanceState)
    
            lifecycleScope.launch {
                // Register and download a model
                val modelInfo = RunAnywhere.registerModel(
                    name = "Qwen 0.5B",
                    url = "https://huggingface.co/Qwen/Qwen2.5-0.5B-Instruct-GGUF/resolve/main/qwen2.5-0.5b-instruct-q8_0.gguf",
                    framework = InferenceFramework.LLAMA_CPP
                )
                modelId = modelInfo.id
    
                // Download with progress tracking
                RunAnywhere.downloadModel(modelInfo.id).collect { progress ->
                    updateProgress((progress.progress * 100).toInt())
                }
    
                // Load and generate
                RunAnywhere.loadLLMModel(modelInfo.id)
    
                val result = RunAnywhere.generate(
                    prompt = "Explain quantum computing in simple terms",
                    options = LLMGenerationOptions(
                        maxTokens = 200,
                        temperature = 0.7f
                    )
                )
    
                showResponse(result.text)
                Log.d("LLM", "Generated in ${result.latencyMs}ms at ${result.tokensPerSecond} tok/s")
            }
        }
    }
    

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/quick-start#step-by-step-guide)

Step-by-Step Guide
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/quick-start#1-initialize-the-sdk)

1\. Initialize the SDK

Initialize RunAnywhere once in your `Application.onCreate()`:

Copy

Ask AI

    RunAnywhere.initialize(
        apiKey = "your-api-key",       // Optional for development mode
        baseURL = null,                // Uses default API endpoint
        environment = SDKEnvironment.DEVELOPMENT
    )
    

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/quick-start#environment-options)

Environment Options

| Environment | Log Level | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `DEVELOPMENT` | Debug | Full logging, local testing |
| `STAGING` | Info | Staging backend, moderate logging |
| `PRODUCTION` | Warning | Production backend, minimal logging |

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/quick-start#2-register-a-model)

2\. Register a Model

Register models from HuggingFace or any direct URL:

Copy

Ask AI

    val modelInfo = RunAnywhere.registerModel(
        name = "Qwen 0.5B",
        url = "https://huggingface.co/.../model.gguf",
        framework = InferenceFramework.LLAMA_CPP
    )
    

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/quick-start#3-download-the-model)

3\. Download the Model

Download with progress tracking using Kotlin Flows:

Copy

Ask AI

    RunAnywhere.downloadModel(modelInfo.id).collect { progress ->
        when (progress.state) {
            DownloadState.DOWNLOADING -> {
                val percent = (progress.progress * 100).toInt()
                progressBar.progress = percent
            }
            DownloadState.COMPLETED -> {
                showMessage("Download complete!")
            }
            DownloadState.ERROR -> {
                showError(progress.error ?: "Download failed")
            }
        }
    }
    

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/quick-start#4-load-and-generate)

4\. Load and Generate

Copy

Ask AI

    // Load the model into memory
    RunAnywhere.loadLLMModel(modelInfo.id)
    
    // Simple chat
    val response = RunAnywhere.chat("What is 2+2?")
    
    // Or with full metrics
    val result = RunAnywhere.generate(
        prompt = "Write a haiku about coding",
        options = LLMGenerationOptions(maxTokens = 50)
    )
    println("Response: ${result.text}")
    println("Tokens/sec: ${result.tokensPerSecond}")
    

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/quick-start#5-stream-responses)

5\. Stream Responses

For real-time token streaming:

Copy

Ask AI

    RunAnywhere.generateStream("Tell me a story about AI")
        .collect { token ->
            // Display tokens as they arrive
            textView.append(token)
        }
    

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/quick-start#what%E2%80%99s-next)

Package Installation
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Choose the packages based on your feature requirements:

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/react-native/installation#full-installation-all-features)

Full Installation (All Features)

Copy

Ask AI

    npm install @runanywhere/core @runanywhere/llamacpp @runanywhere/onnx
    # or
    yarn add @runanywhere/core @runanywhere/llamacpp @runanywhere/onnx
    

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/react-native/installation#llm-only-text-generation)

LLM Only (Text Generation)

Copy

Ask AI

    npm install @runanywhere/core @runanywhere/llamacpp
    # or
    yarn add @runanywhere/core @runanywhere/llamacpp
    

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/react-native/installation#voice-only-stt/tts)

Voice Only (STT/TTS)

Copy

Ask AI

    npm install @runanywhere/core @runanywhere/onnx
    # or
    yarn add @runanywhere/core @runanywhere/onnx
    

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/react-native/installation#required-peer-dependencies)

Required Peer Dependencies

The SDK uses Nitro Modules for its native bridge and requires file system access for model downloads:

Copy

Ask AI

    # Required: Native bridge layer
    npm install react-native-nitro-modules
    
    # Required: File system access for model downloads
    npm install react-native-fs@^2.20.0 react-native-zip-archive@^6.1.0
    

`react-native-fs` and `react-native-zip-archive` are **required** for model downloads. Without them, you will see: `ERROR: react-native-fs not installed - cannot download models`

Include only the SDK modules you need. Each native module adds to your app size: - **@runanywhere/core**: ~2MB (required) - **@runanywhere/llamacpp**: ~15-25MB (for LLM text generation) - **@runanywhere/onnx**: ~50-70MB (for STT, TTS, and VAD)

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/react-native/installation#package-overview)

Package Overview
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Package | Size | Features |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `@runanywhere/core` | ~2MB | Core SDK, model management, events |
| `@runanywhere/llamacpp` | ~15-25MB | LLM text generation (GGUF models) |
| `@runanywhere/onnx` | ~50-70MB | STT, TTS, VAD (ONNX models) |

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/react-native/installation#supported-model-formats)

Supported Model Formats
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Format | Extension | Backend | Use Case |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| GGUF | `.gguf` | LlamaCPP | LLM text generation |
| ONNX | `.onnx` | ONNX Runtime | STT, TTS, VAD |

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/react-native/installation#ios-setup)

iOS Setup
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------

After installing packages, run CocoaPods:

Copy

Ask AI

    cd ios && pod install && cd ..
    

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/react-native/installation#ios-permissions)

iOS Permissions

Add required permissions to your `Info.plist`:

Info.plist

Copy

Ask AI

    <!-- Required for model downloads -->
    <key>NSAppTransportSecurity</key>
    <dict>
      <key>NSAllowsArbitraryLoads</key>
      <true/>
    </dict>
    
    <!-- Required for STT/VAD with microphone -->
    <key>NSMicrophoneUsageDescription</key>
    <string>This app needs microphone access for voice features.</string>
    
    <!-- Required for background audio (optional) -->
    <key>UIBackgroundModes</key>
    <array>
      <string>audio</string>
    </array>
    

`NSMicrophoneUsageDescription` is only required if you‚Äôre using STT or VAD with microphone input.

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/react-native/installation#android-setup)

Android Setup
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Native libraries are automatically downloaded during the Gradle build.

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/react-native/installation#android-build-requirements)

Android Build Requirements

| Requirement | Minimum Version |
| --- | --- |
| Android SDK | compileSdk 36 |
| Android NDK | 27.1.12297006 |
| JDK | 17+ |
| Min API | 24 (Android 7.0+) |

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/react-native/installation#android-permissions)

Android Permissions

Add required permissions to your `AndroidManifest.xml`:

AndroidManifest.xml

Copy

Ask AI

    <!-- Required for model downloads -->
    <uses-permission android:name="android.permission.INTERNET" />
    
    <!-- Required for STT/VAD with microphone -->
    <uses-permission android:name="android.permission.RECORD_AUDIO" />
    
    <!-- Required for large model storage (optional) -->
    <uses-permission android:name="android.permission.WRITE_EXTERNAL_STORAGE"
        android:maxSdkVersion="28" />
    

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/react-native/installation#running-on-physical-device)

Running on Physical Device

1.  **Enable Developer Options:** Settings ‚Üí About Phone ‚Üí Tap ‚ÄúBuild Number‚Äù 7 times
2.  **Enable USB Debugging:** Settings ‚Üí Developer Options ‚Üí USB Debugging
3.  **Connect device:** `adb devices` (should show your device)
4.  **Port forwarding:** `adb reverse tcp:8081 tcp:8081`
5.  **Start Metro:** `npm start`
6.  **Run app:** `npx react-native run-android`

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/react-native/installation#proguard-rules)

ProGuard Rules

If using ProGuard/R8 minification, add these rules to `proguard-rules.pro`:

proguard-rules.pro

Copy

Ask AI

    -keep class com.runanywhere.** { *; }
    -keepclassmembers class com.runanywhere.** { *; }
    -keep class ai.runanywhere.** { *; }
    

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/react-native/installation#troubleshooting-installation)

Troubleshooting Installation
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/react-native/installation#ios-pod-install-fails)

iOS: Pod Install Fails

Copy

Ask AI

    # Clean and reinstall pods
    cd ios
    rm -rf Pods Podfile.lock
    pod cache clean --all
    pod install
    cd ..
    

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/react-native/installation#android-native-library-not-found)

Android: Native Library Not Found

This error typically occurs when running on an emulator:

Copy

Ask AI

    dlopen failed: library "librunanywherecore.so" not found
    

**Solution:** Use a physical ARM64 Android device. Emulators are not supported. If using a physical device:

Copy

Ask AI

    # Clean and rebuild
    cd android
    ./gradlew clean
    cd ..
    npx react-native run-android
    

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/react-native/installation#android-%E2%80%9Chermesenabled%E2%80%9D-property-not-found)

Android: ‚ÄúhermesEnabled‚Äù Property Not Found

**Solution:** Copy the gradle.properties example file:

Copy

Ask AI

    cp android/gradle.properties.example android/gradle.properties
    

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/react-native/installation#android-%E2%80%9Cunable-to-load-script%E2%80%9D-on-device)

Android: ‚ÄúUnable to load script‚Äù on Device

**Solution:** Set up port forwarding for Metro bundler:

Copy

Ask AI

    adb reverse tcp:8081 tcp:8081
    

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/react-native/installation#android-grey-screen-after-launch)

Android: Grey Screen After Launch

**Solution:** Metro bundler may have stopped. Restart it:

Copy

Ask AI

    npm start
    

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/react-native/installation#metro-module-resolution-issues)

Metro: Module Resolution Issues

Copy

Ask AI

    # Reset Metro bundler cache
    npx react-native start --reset-cache
    

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/react-native/installation#both-platforms-fresh-build)

Both Platforms: Fresh Build

Copy

Ask AI

    # Complete clean build
    rm -rf node_modules
    npm install
    cd ios && pod install && cd ..
    npx react-native run-ios  # or run-android
    

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/react-native/installation#native-binary-sizes)

Native Binary Sizes
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Framework | iOS (xcframework) | Android (so) |
| --- | --- | --- |
| RACommons | ~2MB | ~2MB |
| RABackendLLAMACPP | ~15-25MB | ~15-25MB |
| RABackendONNX | ~50-70MB | ~50-70MB |

The ONNX backend is significantly larger due to the ONNX Runtime library. If you only need LLM text generation, consider installing just `@runanywhere/llamacpp` to reduce app size.

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/react-native/installation#next-steps)

Next Steps
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[Quick Start\
-----------\
\
Initialize the SDK and run your first inference ‚Üí](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/react-native/quick-start)

[Introduction](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/react-native/introduction)
[Quick Start](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/react-native/quick-start)

‚åòI

Swift SDK

Introduction

On this page

*   [Overview](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/swift/introduction#overview)

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/swift/introduction#overview)

Overview
------------------------------------------------------------------------

The **RunAnywhere Swift SDK** is a production-grade, on-device AI SDK for Apple platforms. It enables developers to run AI models directly on Apple devices without requiring network connectivity for inference, ensuring minimal latency and maximum privacy for your users. The SDK provides a unified interface to multiple AI capabilities:

[LLM\
---\
\
Text generation with streaming support and structured output](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/swift/llm/chat)
[STT\
---\
\
Speech-to-text transcription with multiple backends](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/swift/stt/transcribe)
[TTS\
---\
\
Neural and system voice synthesis](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/swift/tts/synthesize)
[VAD\
---\
\
Real-time voice activity detection](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/swift/vad)

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/swift/introduction#key-capabilities)

Key Capabilities
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   **Multi-backend architecture** ‚Äì Choose from LlamaCPP (GGUF models), ONNX Runtime, or Apple Foundation Models
*   **Metal acceleration** ‚Äì GPU-accelerated inference on Apple Silicon
*   **Event-driven design** ‚Äì Subscribe to SDK events for reactive UI updates
*   **Production-ready** ‚Äì Built-in analytics, logging, device registration, and model lifecycle management

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/swift/introduction#core-philosophy)

Core Philosophy
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

On-Device First

All AI inference runs locally, ensuring low latency and data privacy. Once models are downloaded, no network connection is required for inference.

Plugin Architecture

Backend engines are optional modules‚Äîinclude only what you need. This keeps your app binary size minimal.

Privacy by Design

Audio and text data never leaves the device unless explicitly configured. Only anonymous analytics are collected by default.

Event-Driven

Subscribe to SDK events for reactive UI updates and observability. Track generation progress, model loading, and errors in real-time.

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/swift/introduction#features)

Features
------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/swift/introduction#language-models-llm)

Language Models (LLM)

*   On-device text generation with streaming support
*   Structured output generation with `Generatable` protocol
*   System prompts and customizable generation parameters
*   Support for thinking/reasoning models with token extraction
*   Multiple framework backends (LlamaCPP, Apple Foundation Models)

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/swift/introduction#speech-to-text-stt)

Speech-to-Text (STT)

*   Real-time streaming transcription
*   Batch audio transcription
*   Multi-language support
*   Whisper-based models via ONNX Runtime

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/swift/introduction#text-to-speech-tts)

Text-to-Speech (TTS)

*   Neural voice synthesis with ONNX models
*   System voices via AVSpeechSynthesizer
*   Streaming audio generation for long text
*   Customizable voice, pitch, rate, and volume

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/swift/introduction#voice-activity-detection-vad)

Voice Activity Detection (VAD)

*   Energy-based speech detection
*   Configurable sensitivity thresholds
*   Real-time audio stream processing

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/swift/introduction#voice-agent-pipeline)

Voice Agent Pipeline

*   Full VAD ‚Üí STT ‚Üí LLM ‚Üí TTS orchestration
*   Complete voice conversation flow
*   Streaming and batch processing modes

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/swift/introduction#model-management)

Model Management

*   Automatic model discovery and catalog sync
*   Download with progress tracking (download, extract, validate stages)
*   In-memory model storage with file system caching
*   Framework-specific model assignment

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/swift/introduction#system-requirements)

System Requirements
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Platform | Minimum Version |
| --- | --- |
| iOS | 17.0+ |
| macOS | 14.0+ |
| tvOS | 17.0+ |
| watchOS | 10.0+ |

**Swift Version:** 5.9+ **Xcode:** 15.2+

Some optional modules have higher runtime requirements: - Apple Foundation Models (`RunAnywhereAppleAI`): iOS 26+ / macOS 26+ at runtime

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/swift/introduction#sdk-modules)

SDK Modules
------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Module | Purpose |
| --- | --- |
| `RunAnywhere` | Core SDK (required) |
| `RunAnywhereLlamaCPP` | LLM text generation with GGUF models |
| `RunAnywhereONNX` | STT/TTS/VAD via ONNX Runtime |

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/swift/introduction#next-steps)

synthesize()

Synthesize text into audio using on-device neural TTS models.

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/tts/synthesize#basic-synthesis)

Basic Synthesis
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Copy

Ask AI

    // Load a TTS voice first
    RunAnywhere.loadTTSVoice("en-us-default")
    
    // Synthesize text to audio
    val output = RunAnywhere.synthesize(
        text = "Hello, welcome to RunAnywhere!",
        options = TTSOptions(rate = 1.0f, pitch = 1.0f)
    )
    
    // Play the audio
    val audioTrack = createAudioTrack(output.format, output.audioData)
    audioTrack.play()
    

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/tts/synthesize#simple-speak-api)

Simple Speak API
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

For convenience, use `speak()` which handles synthesis and playback:

Copy

Ask AI

    // Speak text aloud (handles audio playback automatically)
    val result = RunAnywhere.speak(
        text = "Hello, this is a test message",
        options = TTSOptions(rate = 1.0f)
    )
    
    println("Duration: ${result.duration}s")
    

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/tts/synthesize#ttsoutput)

TTSOutput
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------

The synthesis result object:

| Property | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `audioData` | `ByteArray` | Synthesized audio bytes |
| `format` | `AudioFormat` | Audio format (PCM, WAV, etc.) |
| `duration` | `Double` | Duration in seconds |
| `phonemeTimestamps` | `List<TTSPhonemeTimestamp>?` | Phoneme timing |
| `metadata` | `TTSSynthesisMetadata` | Processing metrics |

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/tts/synthesize#ttsoptions)

TTSOptions
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Customize voice synthesis:

Copy

Ask AI

    data class TTSOptions(
        val voice: String? = null,        // Voice ID (uses loaded voice if null)
        val language: String = "en-US",   // Language code
        val rate: Float = 1.0f,           // Speed (0.0-2.0)
        val pitch: Float = 1.0f,          // Pitch (0.0-2.0)
        val volume: Float = 1.0f,         // Volume (0.0-1.0)
        val audioFormat: AudioFormat = AudioFormat.PCM,
        val sampleRate: Int = 22050,
        val useSSML: Boolean = false      // Enable SSML markup
    )
    

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/tts/synthesize#example-custom-voice-settings)

Example: Custom Voice Settings
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Copy

Ask AI

    val output = RunAnywhere.synthesize(
        text = "The quick brown fox jumps over the lazy dog.",
        options = TTSOptions(
            rate = 0.8f,    // Slower speech
            pitch = 1.2f,   // Higher pitch
            volume = 0.9f
        )
    )
    

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/tts/synthesize#example-playing-audio-with-audiotrack)

Example: Playing Audio with AudioTrack
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Copy

Ask AI

    suspend fun playAudio(audioData: ByteArray, sampleRate: Int = 22050) {
        val audioTrack = AudioTrack.Builder()
            .setAudioAttributes(
                AudioAttributes.Builder()
                    .setUsage(AudioAttributes.USAGE_MEDIA)
                    .setContentType(AudioAttributes.CONTENT_TYPE_SPEECH)
                    .build()
            )
            .setAudioFormat(
                android.media.AudioFormat.Builder()
                    .setEncoding(android.media.AudioFormat.ENCODING_PCM_16BIT)
                    .setSampleRate(sampleRate)
                    .setChannelMask(android.media.AudioFormat.CHANNEL_OUT_MONO)
                    .build()
            )
            .setBufferSizeInBytes(audioData.size)
            .setTransferMode(AudioTrack.MODE_STATIC)
            .build()
    
        audioTrack.write(audioData, 0, audioData.size)
        audioTrack.play()
    }
    

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/tts/synthesize#example-text-to-speech-viewmodel)

Example: Text-to-Speech ViewModel
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Copy

Ask AI

    class TTSViewModel : ViewModel() {
        private val _isSpeaking = MutableStateFlow(false)
        val isSpeaking: StateFlow<Boolean> = _isSpeaking
    
        init {
            viewModelScope.launch {
                // Load TTS voice on init
                RunAnywhere.loadTTSVoice("en-us-default")
            }
        }
    
        fun speak(text: String) {
            viewModelScope.launch {
                _isSpeaking.value = true
                try {
                    RunAnywhere.speak(text, TTSOptions(rate = 1.0f))
                } finally {
                    _isSpeaking.value = false
                }
            }
        }
    
        fun stopSpeaking() {
            viewModelScope.launch {
                RunAnywhere.stopSpeaking()
                _isSpeaking.value = false
            }
        }
    }
    

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/tts/synthesize#check-speaking-status)

Check Speaking Status
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Copy

Ask AI

    // Check if currently speaking
    val isSpeaking = RunAnywhere.isSpeaking()
    
    // Stop current playback
    RunAnywhere.stopSpeaking()

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/voice-agent#overview)

Overview
------------------------------------------------------------------------

The Voice Agent orchestrates the complete voice interaction pipeline: **VAD ‚Üí STT ‚Üí LLM ‚Üí TTS**. This enables full conversational AI with a single API.

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/voice-agent#configure-voice-agent)

Configure Voice Agent
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Copy

Ask AI

    RunAnywhere.configureVoiceAgent(VoiceAgentConfiguration(
        sttModelId = "whisper-tiny",
        llmModelId = "qwen-0.5b",
        ttsVoiceId = "en-us-default",
        systemPrompt = "You are a helpful assistant. Keep responses brief.",
        interruptionEnabled = true
    ))
    

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/voice-agent#voiceagentconfiguration)

VoiceAgentConfiguration
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Copy

Ask AI

    data class VoiceAgentConfiguration(
        val sttModelId: String,              // Speech-to-text model
        val llmModelId: String,              // Language model
        val ttsVoiceId: String,              // Text-to-speech voice
        val systemPrompt: String? = null,    // LLM system prompt
        val vadConfiguration: VADConfiguration? = null,
        val interruptionEnabled: Boolean = true  // Allow user interruption
    )
    

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/voice-agent#process-voice-turn)

Process Voice Turn
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Process a complete voice turn (listen ‚Üí transcribe ‚Üí respond ‚Üí speak):

Copy

Ask AI

    val audioData = // ... recorded audio from user
    
    val result = RunAnywhere.processVoice(audioData)
    
    println("User said: ${result.transcription}")
    println("AI response: ${result.response}")
    println("Total latency: ${result.totalLatencyMs}ms")
    
    // Play the response audio
    result.audioData?.let { audio ->
        audioPlayer.play(audio)
    }
    

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/voice-agent#voiceagentresult)

VoiceAgentResult
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Property | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `transcription` | `String` | User‚Äôs transcribed speech |
| `response` | `String` | AI‚Äôs text response |
| `audioData` | `ByteArray?` | Synthesized response audio |
| `totalLatencyMs` | `Double` | Total processing time |
| `sttLatencyMs` | `Double` | Speech-to-text time |
| `llmLatencyMs` | `Double` | LLM generation time |
| `ttsLatencyMs` | `Double` | Text-to-speech time |

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/voice-agent#voice-session-event-driven)

Voice Session (Event-Driven)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Start a continuous voice session with event streaming:

Copy

Ask AI

    lifecycleScope.launch {
        RunAnywhere.startVoiceSession()
            .collect { event ->
                when (event) {
                    is VoiceSessionEvent.Listening -> {
                        updateUI("Listening...")
                        showMicrophoneActive()
                    }
                    is VoiceSessionEvent.Transcribed -> {
                        updateUI("You: ${event.text}")
                    }
                    is VoiceSessionEvent.Thinking -> {
                        updateUI("Thinking...")
                        showLoadingIndicator()
                    }
                    is VoiceSessionEvent.Responded -> {
                        updateUI("AI: ${event.text}")
                    }
                    is VoiceSessionEvent.Speaking -> {
                        updateUI("Speaking...")
                    }
                    is VoiceSessionEvent.Idle -> {
                        updateUI("Ready")
                    }
                    is VoiceSessionEvent.Error -> {
                        showError(event.message)
                    }
                }
            }
    }
    

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/voice-agent#voicesessionevent)

VoiceSessionEvent
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Copy

Ask AI

    sealed class VoiceSessionEvent {
        object Listening : VoiceSessionEvent()
        data class Transcribed(val text: String) : VoiceSessionEvent()
        object Thinking : VoiceSessionEvent()
        data class Responded(val text: String) : VoiceSessionEvent()
        object Speaking : VoiceSessionEvent()
        object Idle : VoiceSessionEvent()
        data class Error(val message: String) : VoiceSessionEvent()
    }
    

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/voice-agent#session-control)

Session Control
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Copy

Ask AI

    // Stop the voice session
    RunAnywhere.stopVoiceSession()
    
    // Check if session is active
    val isActive = RunAnywhere.isVoiceSessionActive()
    
    // Clear conversation history
    RunAnywhere.clearVoiceConversation()
    
    // Update system prompt mid-session
    RunAnywhere.setVoiceSystemPrompt("You are now a coding assistant.")
    

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/voice-agent#example-complete-voice-assistant)

Example: Complete Voice Assistant
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Copy

Ask AI

    class VoiceAssistantActivity : AppCompatActivity() {
    
        override fun onCreate(savedInstanceState: Bundle?) {
            super.onCreate(savedInstanceState)
            setContentView(R.layout.activity_voice_assistant)
    
            lifecycleScope.launch {
                // Configure voice agent
                RunAnywhere.configureVoiceAgent(VoiceAgentConfiguration(
                    sttModelId = "whisper-tiny",
                    llmModelId = "qwen-0.5b",
                    ttsVoiceId = "en-us-default",
                    systemPrompt = """
                        You are a helpful voice assistant.
                        Keep responses under 2 sentences.
                        Be friendly and conversational.
                    """.trimIndent()
                ))
    
                // Check if ready
                if (!RunAnywhere.isVoiceAgentReady()) {
                    showMessage("Loading models...")
                    RunAnywhere.initializeVoiceAgentWithLoadedModels()
                }
            }
    
            startButton.setOnClickListener {
                startVoiceSession()
            }
    
            stopButton.setOnClickListener {
                lifecycleScope.launch {
                    RunAnywhere.stopVoiceSession()
                }
            }
        }
    
        private fun startVoiceSession() {
            lifecycleScope.launch {
                RunAnywhere.startVoiceSession()
                    .collect { event ->
                        runOnUiThread {
                            when (event) {
                                is VoiceSessionEvent.Listening -> {
                                    statusText.text = "üé§ Listening..."
                                    micButton.setColorFilter(Color.RED)
                                }
                                is VoiceSessionEvent.Transcribed -> {
                                    transcriptionText.text = event.text
                                }
                                is VoiceSessionEvent.Thinking -> {
                                    statusText.text = "ü§î Thinking..."
                                }
                                is VoiceSessionEvent.Responded -> {
                                    responseText.text = event.text
                                }
                                is VoiceSessionEvent.Speaking -> {
                                    statusText.text = "üîä Speaking..."
                                }
                                is VoiceSessionEvent.Idle -> {
                                    statusText.text = "Ready"
                                    micButton.clearColorFilter()
                                }
                                is VoiceSessionEvent.Error -> {
                                    Toast.makeText(this@VoiceAssistantActivity,
                                        event.message, Toast.LENGTH_SHORT).show()
                                }
                            }
                        }
                    }
            }
        }
    }
    

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/voice-agent#component-states)

Component States
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Check individual component readiness:

Copy

Ask AI

    val states = RunAnywhere.voiceAgentComponentStates()
    println("STT ready: ${states.sttReady}")
    println("LLM ready: ${states.llmReady}")
    println("TTS ready: ${states.ttsReady}")
    println("VAD ready: ${states.vadReady}")
    

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/voice-agent#performance-optimization)

Performance Optimization
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Minimize total latency:** Use smaller models (whisper-tiny, 0.5B LLM), enable streaming for both LLM and TTS, and preload all models at app startup.

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/voice-agent#typical-latencies-pixel-7)

Typical Latencies (Pixel 7)

| Stage | Latency |
| --- | --- |
| STT | 200-400ms for 5s audio |
| LLM | 150-300ms for 50 tokens |
| TTS | 100-200ms for short responses |
| **Total round-trip** | **500-900ms** |

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/voice-agent#related)

Related
----------------------------------------------------------------------

[VAD\

\

[STT\

\
Speech-to-Text](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/stt/transcribe)
[TTS\
---\
\
Text-to-Speech](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/kotlin/tts/synthesize)

# chat() - RunAnywhere Documentation

[Skip to main content](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/react-native/llm/chat#content-area)

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/react-native/llm/chat#overview)

Overview
---------------------------------------------------------------------------

The `chat()` method provides the simplest way to interact with an LLM. It takes a prompt and returns just the response text, making it perfect for quick integrations.

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/react-native/llm/chat#basic-usage)

Basic Usage
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Copy

Ask AI

    import { RunAnywhere } from '@runanywhere/core'
    
    // Simple question
    const response = await RunAnywhere.chat('What is the capital of France?')
    console.log(response) // "Paris is the capital of France."
    
    // Follow-up (stateless - each call is independent)
    const answer = await RunAnywhere.chat('What is 2 + 2?')
    console.log(answer) // "4"
    

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/react-native/llm/chat#api-reference)

API Reference
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Copy

Ask AI

    await RunAnywhere.chat(prompt: string): Promise<string>
    

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/react-native/llm/chat#parameters)

Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `prompt` | `string` | The user‚Äôs message or question |

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/react-native/llm/chat#returns)

Returns

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `Promise<string>` | The generated response text |

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/react-native/llm/chat#throws)

Throws

| Error Code | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `notInitialized` | SDK not initialized |
| `modelNotLoaded` | No LLM model loaded |
| `generationFailed` | Generation failed |

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/react-native/llm/chat#examples)

Examples
---------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/react-native/llm/chat#simple-q&a)

Simple Q&A

Copy

Ask AI

    const capital = await RunAnywhere.chat('What is the capital of Japan?')
    // "Tokyo is the capital of Japan."
    
    const math = await RunAnywhere.chat('Calculate 15% of 200')
    // "15% of 200 is 30."
    
    const translation = await RunAnywhere.chat('Translate "Hello" to Spanish')
    // "Hola"
    

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/react-native/llm/chat#react-component)

React Component

ChatComponent.tsx

Copy

Ask AI

    import React, { useState } from 'react'
    import { View, TextInput, Button, Text } from 'react-native'
    import { RunAnywhere } from '@runanywhere/core'
    
    export function ChatComponent() {
      const [input, setInput] = useState('')
      const [response, setResponse] = useState('')
      const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false)
    
      const handleSend = async () => {
        if (!input.trim()) return
    
        setLoading(true)
        try {
          const answer = await RunAnywhere.chat(input)
          setResponse(answer)
        } catch (error) {
          setResponse('Error: ' + (error as Error).message)
        } finally {
          setLoading(false)
        }
      }
    
      return (
        <View style={{ padding: 16 }}>
          <TextInput
            value={input}
            onChangeText={setInput}
            placeholder="Ask anything..."
            style={{ borderWidth: 1, padding: 8, marginBottom: 8 }}
          />
          <Button title={loading ? 'Thinking...' : 'Send'} onPress={handleSend} disabled={loading} />
          {response ? <Text style={{ marginTop: 16 }}>{response}</Text> : null}
        </View>
      )
    }
    

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/react-native/llm/chat#with-error-handling)

With Error Handling

Copy

Ask AI

    import { RunAnywhere, isSDKError, SDKErrorCode } from '@runanywhere/core'
    
    async function askQuestion(question: string): Promise<string> {
      try {
        return await RunAnywhere.chat(question)
      } catch (error) {
        if (isSDKError(error)) {
          switch (error.code) {
            case SDKErrorCode.notInitialized:
              throw new Error('Please initialize the SDK first')
            case SDKErrorCode.modelNotLoaded:
              throw new Error('Please load a model first')
            default:
              throw new Error('AI error: ' + error.message)
          }
        }
        throw error
      }
    }
    
    // Usage
    const response = await askQuestion('What is AI?')
    

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/react-native/llm/chat#chat-vs-generate)

Chat vs Generate
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Feature | `chat()` | `generate()` |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Return type | `string` | `GenerationResult` |
| Metrics | No  | Yes (tokens, latency, tok/s) |
| Options | No  | Yes (maxTokens, temperature, etc.) |
| System prompt | No  | Yes |
| Use case | Quick prototyping | Production apps |

Use `chat()` for quick prototyping and simple interactions. Switch to `generate()` when you need performance metrics, custom options, or system prompts.

[‚Äã](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/react-native/llm/chat#related)

Related
-------------------------------------------------------------------------

Full generation with options and metrics](https://docs.runanywhere.ai/react-native/llm/generate)
